makha makhadhara mātṛbaddhadāmannavanītapriya ballavīgaṇeśa 
aghabakavṛṣakeśipūtanānta triśirovālidaśāsyabhedakārin  NarP 
narakamuravināśa bāṇadoḥ kṛttripurārījya sudāmamitra sevya 
bhavataraṇivahitrapādapadma prakaṭaiśvarya purāṇa pūrṇabāho  NarP 
bahujanisukṛtāpya maṅgalārha śrutivedya śrutidhāma śāntaśuddha 
tava varada vareṇyamaṅghriyugmaṃ śaraṇaṃ prāptamaghārditaṃ prapāhi  NarP 
nahi mama gatidaṃ purāṇapuṃso 'nyaditi prārthanayā prasīda'medya  NarP 
iti stuto jagannātho bhaktyā devena śaṃbhunā 
āvirbabhūva sahasā mādhavo bhaktavatsalaḥ  NarP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā daṇḍavadbhūmau nipapāta haro harim 
punarutthāya viprendra nanāma vidhṛtāñjaliḥ  NarP 
tamuvāca hṛṣīkeśaḥ praṇataṃ bhūtanāyakam 
varaṃ vṛṇu pradāsye 'haṃ saṃtuṣṭaḥ stotratastava  NarP 
tacchrutvā bhagavadvākyaṃ bhūteśo brahyahatyayā 
pīḍitātmā jagādedaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ harim  NarP 
icchāmi vasituṃ kṣetre tava cakragadādhara 
tvatkṣetrasīmābāhyasthā brahmahatyā yadīkṣyate  NarP 
kṣetradānena kāruṇyaṃ kuru me garuḍadhvaja 
mama nirgamane brahmahatyā māṃ punareṣyati  NarP 
tvatkṣetre saṃsthito 'haṃ tu pūjāṃ prāpsye jagattraye 
ityuktvā hyabhavattūṣṇīṃ devadevaṃ vṛṣadhvajaḥ  NarP 
tatheti pratipede ca kṣīrasāgarajāpriyaḥ 
tataḥ prabhṛti viprendra śaivaṃ kṣetraṃ nigadyate  NarP 
kṣetraṃ tu keśavasyedaṃ purāṇaṃ kavayo viduḥ 
kṛpayā saṃparītasya mādhavasya dvijottama  NarP 
netrābhyāṃ nirgataṃ vāri tena bindusaro 'bhavat 
mādhavasyājñayā tatra sasnau devo vṛṣadhvajaḥ  NarP 
snātamātre hare tattu kapālaṃ pāṇito 'patat 
kapālamocanaṃ nāma tattīrthaṃ khyātimāgatam  NarP 
bindumādhavanāmāsau datvā svaṃ dhāma śūline 
bhaktibhāvena śaṃbhustu nibaddhastatra saṃsthitaḥ  NarP 
yaṃ tu brahmādayo devāḥ svaḥsthāḥ paśyati sarvadā 
sūryāyutasamaprakhya digaṃbaraniṣevitam  NarP 
vighnāni śūlinā kānta kṛtānyasya niṣevaṇe 
yairvighnairabhibhūtāstu stutvā viṣṇuṃ śivārcakāḥ  NarP 
sarve lokāḥ sthitā hyatra śivaḥ kāśīti cintakāḥ 
śivasya cintanādvipra śaivāḥ sarve nirākulāḥ  NarP 
prayānti śivalokaṃ vaijarāmṛtyuvivarjitam 
bahupuṇyayutāḥ saṃto nivasaṃttayatra nīrujaḥ  NarP 
yajñaśiṣṭāśinaḥ kāśīkānta ṛddhisamanvitāḥ 
nātra snānaṃ praśaṃsaṃti na japaṃ na surārcanam  NarP 
nāpi dānaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha muktvaikaṃ dehapātanam 
mṛtyuṃ prātyuṃ naraḥ kāmaṃ kṛtakṛtyo bhaveddhruvan  NarP 
seyamāsāditā viprara purī prāsādasaṃkulā 
bhoginīmapi mokṣāya kiṃ punarvratadhāriṇām  NarP 
nikṣipyatāmiyaṃ bālā kāśīśasyeha mandire 
viyojitā tu yā pūrvaṃ tena duṣṭena rakṣasā  NarP 
ātmanaḥ suratārthāya kumārī niyamānvitā 
eṣa prabhāvo 'pi hitaḥ kṣetrasyāsya dvijotma  NarP 
vinaśyantīha karmāṇi śubhānyapyaśubhāni ca 
bhūtavyabhaviṣyāṇi jñānājñānakṛtāni ca  NarP 
eṣā purī karmavināśanāya kṛṣṇena pūrvaṃ hi vinirmitābhūt 
yasyāṃ mṛtā duḥkhamanantamugraṃ bhuñjanti martyā yamayātanāṃ no  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite kāṣṭhīlopākhyāne rākṣasīcarite kāśīvarṇanaṃ nāma ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
kāṣṭhīlovāca
bhāryāyāstadvacaḥ śrutvā rākṣasyā dharmasaṃmitam 
pṛṣṭhātkaroṇurūpiṇyāḥ sakanyo 'vātaraddvijaḥ  NarP 
avatīrṇe dvije sābhūtsurūpā pramadā punaḥ 
kṣapācarī kṣapānāthavaktrā pīnonnatastanī  NarP 
sā kumārī tataḥ prāpya nagaraṃ svapituḥ śubham 
bāhyarakṣāsthita prāptaṃ purapālamuvāca ha  NarP 
gaccha tvaṃ nṛpateḥ pārśvaṃ piturmama purādhipa 
brūhi māṃ samanuprāptāṃ ratnaśālāṃ purā hṛtām  NarP 
ratnāvaliṃ ratnabhūtāṃ sudyumnasya mahīkṣituḥ 
talpasthā rakṣasā rātrau svapurasthā hṛtā dvija  NarP 
punaḥ sā samanuprāptā jīvamānākṣatā pitaḥ 
samāśvasihi śokaṃ tvaṃ mā kṛthā matkṛte kvacit  NarP 
aviplutāsmi rājendra gāṅgā āpa ivāmalāḥ 
tava kīrtikarī tadvanmātuḥ sauśīlyasūcikā  NarP 
tatkumārīvacaḥ śrutvā purāpālastvarānvitaḥ 
abāhuriti vikhyātaḥ prāptaḥ sudyumrasannidhau  NarP 
kṛtapraṇāmaḥ saṃpṛṣṭaḥ prāha rājānamādarāt 
rājannupāgatā naṣṭā dihitā tava mānada  NarP 
ratnāvalīti vikhyātā sastrīkadvidajasaṃyutā 
purabāhye sthitā dṛṣṭā mayā jñātā na cābhavat  NarP 
tayāhaṃ preritaḥ prāgāṃ tvāṃ vijñāpayituṃ prabho 
aviplutāhaṃ vadati māṃ jānātu samāgatām  NarP 
pitaraṃ mama satkṛtyai nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
tadadbhutaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā purapālasya tatkṣaṇāt  NarP 
sāmātyaḥ sakalatrastu sadvijo niryayau nṛpaḥ 
sa tu gatvā purādbrāhye gaṅgātīre vyavasthitām  NarP 
apaśyadbhāskarākārāṃ sastrīkadvijasaṃyutām 
sahaje naiva veṣeṇa bhūṣitāṃ bhūṣaṇapriyām  NarP 
amlānakusumaprakhyāṃ tatpakāñcanasuprabhām 
dūrāddṛṣṭvāntikaṃ gatvā paryaṣvajata bhūpatiḥ  NarP 
pitaraṃ sāpi saṃhṛṣṭā samāśliṣya nanāma ha 
tataśca mātrā saṃgamya hṛṣṭayā harṣitāntarā  NarP 
prāha vākyaṃ viśālākṣī saṃbodhya pitaraṃ nṛpam 
suptāhaṃ ratnaśālāyāṃ sakhībhiḥ parivāritā  NarP 
udakūkṛtvā śirastātādhautāṅghrirmañcakopari 
cintayatnī bhartṛyogaṃ niśīthe rakṣasā hṛtā  NarP 
sa māṃ gṛhītvā svapuraṃ prāgādarṇavage girau 
nānāratnamaye tatra guhāyāṃ sthāpitā hyaham  NarP 
sa tatrodvahanopāyacintayāntarvyavasthitaḥ 
tasya bhāryā tviyaṃ subhrūryā tiṣṭhati sumadhyamā  NarP 
bibhratī mānuṣaṃ rūpaṃ rākṣasī rākṣasapriyā 
anayā buddhiyogena śaktyā śakrasya bhūpate  NarP 
ghātito viprahastena krūrakarmā patiḥ svakaḥ 
puraiva mama taṃ śailaṃ prāpto devena bhūsuraḥ  NarP 
iyaṃ tu rākṣasī dṛṣṭvā patiṃ svaṃ dharmadūṣakam 
vipreṇa saṃvidaṃ kṛtvā dāṃpatye nijakarmaṇā  NarP 
rūpeṇāpyasya saṃmugdhā ghātayāmāsa rākṣasam 
evaṃ kṛtvā patiṃ vipraṃ hastinīrūpadhāriṇī  NarP 
gṛhītvā vāstukaṃ vittaṃ pṛṣṭhamāropya māmapi 
samāyātātra bhūpāla māmattuṃ tava mandiram  NarP 
anayā rakṣitā rājan rākṣasyārākṣasāttataḥ 
tasmādimāṃ pūjayasva satkṛtyāgrajasaṃyutām  NarP 
asyā evāmumatyā māṃ dehyasmai brāhmaṇāya hi 
anenaikāsanagatā jātā bhartā sa me bhavat  NarP 
yenaikāsanagā nārī bhavedbhartā sa eva hi 
nānya itthaṃ purāṇeṣu śrūyate hyāgameṣvapi  NarP 
asyāḥ pṛṣṭhe niviṣṭāhaṃ prītyā saha dvijanmanā 
dharmata stena madbhartā bhavedeṣā matirmama  NarP 
tasmādimāṃ sāṃtvayitvā śāstrāgamavidhānataḥ 
dehi viprāya māṃ tāta pitamanyaṃ vṛṇe na ca  NarP 
tacchrutvā duhiturvākyaṃ sudyumno bhūpatistadā 
sāṃtvayāmāsa tanvaṅgīṃ rākṣasīṃ praśrayānataḥ  NarP 
sutaiṣā dharmabhītā me tvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gatā 
yadarthaṃ nihataḥ kāntastvayā pūrvataraḥ sati  NarP 
tvadadhīnā tato bhadre jāteyaṃ matsutā kila 
imamicchati bhartāraṃ yo 'yaṃ bhartā kṛtastvayā  NarP 
mayā praṇāmadānābhyāṃ yācitā tvaṃ niśācari 
anumodaya sāhāyye sutāṃ mama sulocane  NarP 
tvadvākyādbhavatu preṣyā matsutā brāhmaṇasya tu 
sāpatnabhāvaṃ tyaktvā tu sutāṃ me paripālaya  NarP 
sutāyā mama bhāryāyā madbalasya janasya ca 
purasya viṣayasyāpi svāminī tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  NarP 
tava vākye sthitā hyeṣā sadaivāpi bhaviṣyati 
etacchruttvā tu vacanaṃ sudyumnasya niśācarī  NarP 
anvamodata śuddhena cetasā sahacāriṇī 
uvāca ca dharāpālaṃ pradānāya kṛtodyamam  NarP 
yadarthaṃ praṇatastvaṃ māṃ sadbhāvena nṛpottama 
tasmāddvitīyā bhāryeyaṃ bhavatvasya dvijanmanaḥ  NarP 
ahaṃ ca bhavatā pūjyā kṛtvārcāṃ devamandire 
sarvaiśca nāgaraiḥ sārddhaṃ phālgune dhavale dale  NarP 
saptāhamutsavaḥ kāryo hyaṣṭamyā ācaturdaśīm 
naṭanartakayuktena gītavādyena bhūriṇā  NarP 
maireyamāṃsaraktādibalibhiścāpi pūjayā 
evaṃ prakurvate tubhyaṃ sadā kṣemakarī hyaham  NarP 
bhaveyaṃ nṛpaśārdūla svaṃ vacaḥ pratipālaya 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasyāḥ sudyumno nṛpatistadā  NarP 
aṅgīcakāra tatsarvaṃ yaduktaṃ prītayā tayā 
pratipanne tu vacasi rājñā tuṣṭā tu rākṣasī  NarP 
uvāca brāhmaṇaṃ premṇā kuru bhāryāmimāmapi 
rājakanyāṃ dvijaśreṣṭha gṛhyoktavidhinā śubhām  NarP 
īrṣyāṃ tyaktvā viśālākṣyā bhavāmyeṣā sahodarī 
rākṣasyā vacaneneha pariṇīya nṛpātmajām  NarP 
bahuvittayutāṃ vipro mahodayapuraṃ yayau 
āruhya kariṇīrūpāṃ rākṣasīṃ kṣaṇamātrataḥ  NarP 
tato mayā śrutaṃ devi bhartā te samupāgataḥ 
dhanaratnasamāyukto bhāryādvayasamanvitaḥ  NarP 
tato 'haṃ bandhuvargeṇa pitṛbhyāṃ ca sakhīgaṇaiḥ 
bahuśo bhartsitā rūkṣairvacanairmarmabhedibhiḥ  NarP 
kathaṃ yāsyasi bhartāraṃ dhanalubdhe śriyā vṛtam 
yastvayā nirddhanaḥ pūrvaṃ parityaktaḥ sudīnavat  NarP 
cañcalānīha vittāni pitryāṇi kila yoṣitām 
kāntārjitāni subhage sthirāṇīti nigadyate  NarP 
paruṣairvacanairyastu kṣiptastadbhāṣaṇaṃ katham 
bhaviṣyati praveśo 'pi duṣkarastasya veśmani  NarP 
gatāyā api te tatra śayanaṃ patinā saha 
bhaviṣyati durācāre sukhadaṃ na kadācana  NarP 
lokāpavādādyadi cedgrahīṣyati patistava 
tvāṃ snehahīnacittastu na kadācinmiliṣyati  NarP 
nedṛśaṃ duḥkhadaṃ kiñcidyādṛśaṃ dūracittayoḥ 
daṃpakatyormilanaṃ loke vaikalyakaraṇaṃ mahat  NarP 
evaṃ bahuvidhā vācaḥ śṛṇvānā bandhubhāṣitāḥ 
adhomukhyasrupūrṇākṣī babhūvāhaṃ suduḥkhitā  NarP 
cetasārcitayaṃ cāhaṃ pūrvalobhena muhyatī 
na dattaṃ kaṅkaṇaṃ pāṇerna dattaṃ kaṭisūtrakam  NarP 
na cāpi nūpure datte yena tuṣṭiṃ vrajetpatiḥ 
dhanajīvitayoḥ svāmī bhartā lokeṣu gīyate  NarP 
tanmayāpahṛtaṃ vittaṃ bhavitrī kā gatirmama 
kathaṃ yāsyāmi tadveśma kathaṃ saṃbhāṣaye punaḥ  NarP 
yo mayā duṣṭayā tyaktaḥ sa pratyeti kathaṃ hi mām 
evaṃ viciṃye yādaddhṛdayena vidūyatā  NarP 
veṣṭitā bandhuvargeṇa tāvaddolā samāgatā 
chatreṇa śaśivarṇena śobhamānā sukomalā  NarP 
āstṛtā rāṅkavaiḥ pīnaiḥ puruṣorvidhṛtāṃsakaiḥ 
te samāgatya puruṣāḥ procurmāmasakṛcchabhe  NarP 
ākāritāsi patyā te vraja śīghraṃ mudānvitā 
dhanaratnayuto bhartā saddhibhāryaḥ samāgataḥ  NarP 
praviṣṭamātreṇa gṛhe tvāmānetuṃ varānane 
preṣitāḥ satvaraṃ patyā saṃsthitāṃ pitṛveśmani  NarP 
tato 'haṃ vrīḍitā devi bhartustadvīkṣya ceṣṭitam 
naivottaramadāṃ tebhyaḥ kiñcinmaunaṃ samāsthitā  NarP 
tato 'haṃ bandhuvargeṇa bhūyobhūyaḥ prabodhitā 
āhūtā svāminā gaccha sammānena tadantikam  NarP 
svāminākāritā patnī yā na yāti tadantikam 
sā tu dhvāṅkṣī bhavetputri janmāni daśa pañca ca  NarP 
evamuktvā samāśvāsya māṃ gṛhītvā tvarānvitāḥ 
dolāmāropya gaccheti procuḥ snigdhā muhurmurhuḥ  NarP 
tataste puruṣā dolāṃ nidhāyāṃseṣu satvaram 
jagmurmahodayapuraṃ yatra tiṣṭhati me patiḥ  NarP 
dṛṣṭaṃ mayā gṛhaṃ tasya sarvataḥ kāñcanāvṛtam 
āsanīyaiśca bhojyaiśca dhanairvastrairyutaṃ tataḥ  NarP 
atha sā rākṣasī devī sā cāpi nṛpanandinī 
prītyā ca bhaktyā kurutāṃ praṇatiṃ mama sundari  NarP 
tatastābhyāmamahaṃ premṇā yathārhamabhipūjitā 
bhartṛvākyena saṃprītā snātvābhujaṃ tathāhṛtā  NarP 
tato 'stasamayātpaścādbhartā cāhūya satvaram 
pariṣvajya ciraṃ dorbhyāṃ paryaṅke saṃnyaveśayat  NarP 
tato niśācarīṃ rājaputrīṃ cāhūya so 'bravīt 
bhaktyā yuvābhyāṃ kartavyamasyāścaraṇasevanam  NarP 
iyaṃ prākkālikī bhāryā jyeṣṭhā ca yuvayordbhuvam 
patyurvākyāttatastābhyāṃ gṛhītau caraṇau mama  NarP 
sāpatnabhāvajāmīrṣyāṃ parityajya sulocane 
tataḥ preṣyānsamāhūya bhartā me vākyamabravīt  NarP 
yatkiñcidrakṣasaḥ pārśvānmayā prāptaṃ purā vasu 
sutāmudvahato rājño yacca labdhaṃ mayākhilam  NarP 
tatsarvaṃ bhaktibhāvena samānayata mā ciram 
iyaṃ hi svāminī prāptā tasya vittasya kiṅkarāḥ  NarP 
tadvākyātsahasā preṣyaiḥ samānītaṃ dhanaṃ śubhe 
bhartā samarpayāmāsa prītyā yukto 'khilaṃ tadā  NarP 
satkṛtya bhūṣaṇairvastraikhyalīkena cetasā 
ubhayostatra paśyantyo rākṣasīrājakanyayoḥ  NarP 
paryaṅkasthāṃ pariṣvajya māṃ cuñcubādhare śubhe 
taddṛṣṭvā cādbhutaṃ bharturdehavittasamarpaṇam  NarP 
ullāsakaraṇa vākyaṃ kareṇa kucapīḍanam 
chinnā gauriva khaṅgena gatāḥ prāṇā mamābhavan  NarP 
tato 'haṃ yamanirddiṣṭāṃ prāptā narakayātanām 
tāmatītya suduḥkhārtā kāṣṭhīlā cābhavaṃ śubhe  NarP 
yāsyāmi punarevāhaṃ tiryagyoniṃ sahasraśaḥ 
yā bharturnāpayedvittaṃ jīvitaṃ ca śubhānane  NarP 
sāpīdṛśīmavasthā vai yāsyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ 
evaṃ jñātvāniśaṃ rakṣetpatyurvittaṃ ca jīvitam  NarP 
patirmātā pitā vittaṃ jīvitaṃ ca gururgatiḥ  NarP 
prayāti nārī bahubhiḥ supuṇyaiḥ sahaiva bhartrā svaśarīradāhāt 
viṣṇoḥ padaṃ vittaśarīralubdhā prayāti yāmīṃ ca kuyonipīḍām  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite kāṣṭhīlācaritaṃ nāma triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
vasiṣṭha uvāca
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasyāḥ kāṣṭhīlāyāḥ śucismite 
sandhyāvalī nāma bhṛśaṃ tāmuvāca ha sādaram  NarP 
tvadvākyādvismayo jātaḥ kāṣṭhīle sāṃprataṃ mama 
kathaṃ dṛṣṭā mayā tvaṃ ca yāsyantī kutsitāṃ gatim  NarP 
karmaṇā kena te muktirbhavetkutsitayonitaḥ 
tanme vada viśālāṅge tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā duḥkhitā hyaham  NarP 
māṃsapiṇḍopamaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ navanītopamaṃ śubhe 
śarīraṃ tava saṃvīkṣya tayā me jāyate hṛdi  NarP 
kāṣṭhīlovāca
pṛthivīṃ dāsyase subhru sakalāmapi matkṛte 
tathāpi naiva mucyeyaṃ sadyaḥ kutsitayonitaḥ  NarP 
yena puṇyena subhage mucyeyaṃ karmabandhanāt 
tannirdiśāmi sumahadgatidaṃ tvaṃ niśāmaya  NarP 
yaścāyaṃ māghamāsastu sarvamāsottamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
yasmin krośanti pāpāni brahmahatyādikāni ca  NarP 
durlabho māghamāso vai durllabhaṃ janma mānuṣam 
durllabhaṃ coṣasi snānaṃ durlabhaṃ kṛṣṇasevanam  NarP 
durlabho vāsaro viṣṇorvidhinā samupoṣitaḥ 
devaistejaḥ parikṣiptaṃ māghamāse svakaṃ jale  NarP 
tasmājjalaṃ māghamāse pāvanaṃ hi viśeṣataḥ 
nedṛśī saṃgare śūrairgatiḥ prāpyeta saukhyadā  NarP 
yādṛśī plavane prātaḥ prāpyate niyamasthitaiḥ 
sarittaḍāgavāpīṣu snāne sattamamīritam  NarP 
kūpabhāṇḍajalairmadhyaṃ jaghanyaṃ vahnitāpitaiḥ 
na saukhyairlabhyate puṇyaṃ duḥkhairevāpyate tu tat  NarP 
dharmmasevārthakaṃ snānaṃ nāṅganairmalyahetukam 
homārthaṃ sevanaṃ vahnerna ca śītādihānaye  NarP 
yāvannodayate sūryastāvatsnānaṃ vidhīyate 
ācchādite ghanairvyomni hyudgamiṣyantamarthayet  NarP 
abhāve saridādīnāṃ navakuṃbhasthitaṃ jalam 
vāyunā tāḍitaṃ rātrau snāne gaṅgāsamaṃ viduḥ  NarP 
māghasnāyī varārohe durgatiṃ naiva paśyati 
tannāsti pātakaṃ yattu māghasnānaṃ na śodhayet  NarP 
agnipraveśādadhikaṃ māghoṣasyeva majjanam 
jīvatā bhujyate duḥkhaṃ mṛtena bahulaṃ sukham  NarP 
etasmātkāraṇādbhadre māghasnānaṃ viśiṣyate 
ahanyahani dātavyāstilāḥ śarkarayānvitāḥ  NarP 
meghapuṃṣpopapannena sahānnena sumadhyame 
yāvakaiścaiva hotavyā gavyasarpiḥ samanvitaiḥ  NarP 
mādhyāṃ snānasamāptai tu dadyādviprāya ṣaḍrasam 
sūryo me prīyatāṃ devo viṣṇumūrtirnirañjanaḥ  NarP 
vāsāṃsi dvijayugmāya sa saptānnāni cārpayet 
triṃśacca modakā deyāstilānnāḥ śarkarāmayāḥ  NarP 
bhāgāstrayastilānāṃ tu caturthaḥ śarkarāṃśakaḥ 
tāṃbūlādīni bhogyāni bhaktyādakadyādvidhānavit  NarP 
srotomukhaḥ sariti cānyatra bhāskarasaṃmukhaḥ 
snāyādāvāhya tīrthāni gaṅgādīnya karmaṇḍalāt  NarP 
yadanekajanurjanyaṃ yajjñānājñānataḥ kṛtam 
tvattejasā hataṃ cāstu tattu pāpaṃ sahasradhā  NarP 
divākara jagannātha prabhākara namo 'stu te 
paripūrṇaṃ kuruṣvedaṃ māghasnānaṃ mamācyuta  NarP 
tīrthasnāyī varārohe māghasnāyī phalālpakaḥ 
tīrthasnānādiyātsvargaṃ māghasnānātparaṃ padam  NarP 
māghasya dhavale pakṣe bhavedekādaśī tu yā 
ravivāreṇa saṃyuktā mahāpātakanāśinī  NarP 
vināpi ṛkṣasaṃyogaṃ sā śuklaikādaśī nṛṇām 
vinirdahati pāpāni kunṛpo viṣayaṃ yathā  NarP 
kuputrastu kulaṃ yadvatkubhāryā ca patiṃ yathā 
adharmastu yathā dharmaṃ kumantrī nṛpatiṃ yathā  NarP 
ajñānaṃ ca yathā jñānaṃ kuśaucaṃ śucitāṃ yathā 
yathā hantyanṛtaṃ satyaṃ vādassaṃvādameva ca  NarP 
uṣṇaṃ himamanarthor'thaṃ pāpaṃ kīrtiṃ smayastapaḥ 
yathā rasā mahārogāñchrāddhaṃ saṃketa eva ca  NarP 
tathā duritasaṃghaṃ tu dvādaśī hanti sādhitā 
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ steyaṃ gurvaṅganāgamaḥ  NarP 
mahānti pātakānyetānyāśu hanti harerdinam 
samavetāni caitāni na śāmayati puṣkaram  NarP 
na cāpi naimiṣāraṇyaṃ na kṣetraṃ kurusaṃjñitam 
prabhāso na gayā devi na revā na sarasvatī  NarP 
na gagā yamunā caiva prayāgo na ca devakā 
na sarāṃsi nadāścānye homadānatapāṃsi ca  NarP 
na cānyatsukṛtaṃ subhru purāṇe paṭhyate sphuṭam 
pāpasaṃghavināśāya muktvaikaṃ harivāsaram  NarP 
upoṣaṇātsakṛddevi vinaśyantyagharāśayaḥ 
ekataḥ pṛthivīdānamekato harivāsaram  NarP 
na samaṃ brahmaṇā proktamadhikaṃ harivāsaram 
tasminvarāhavapuṣaṃ kṛtvā devaṃ tu hāṭakam  NarP 
ghaṭopari nave pātre dhṛtvā tāmramaye śubhe 
sarvabījānvite caiva sitavastrāvaguṇṭhite  NarP 
sahiraṇye sudīpāḍhye kṛtapuṣpāvataṃsake 
vidhinā pūjayitvā cakuryājjāgaraṇaṃ vratī  NarP 
prātarviprāya dadyācca vaiṣṇavāya kuṭuṃbine 
tatkuṃbhakroḍasaṃyuktaṃ sanaivedyaparicchadam  NarP 
paścācca pāraṇaṃ kuryāddvijānbhojya suhṛdvṛtaḥ 
evaṃ kṛte varārohe na bhūyo jāyate kvacit  NarP 
bahujanmārjjitaṃ pāpaṃ jñānājñānakṛtaṃ ca yat 
tatsarvaṃ nāśamāyāti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā  NarP 
yathāśāstraṃ mayā tubhyaṃ varṇitā dvādaśī śubhe 
yā sā kṛtā tvayā pūrvamāsīddevyanyajanmani  NarP 
yasyāstavātulā puṣṭirvartate vartayiṣyati 
bharttustava ca putrasya sarvadā sukhadāyinī  NarP 
tasyāstvayā turīyāṃśo deyaścenmahyamādarāt 
tadā prītā gamiṣyāmi tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  NarP 
vittāhrutijaṃ pāpaṃ yadbhūtaṃ mama suṃdari 
tasya pāvanahetuṃ ca turīyāṃśaṃ prayaccha me  NarP 
jīvitenāpi vittena bhartāraṃ vañcayettu yā 
kṛmiyoniśataṃ gatvā pulkasī jāyate tu sā  NarP 
surataṃ yācamānāya patye vittaṃ ca mānini 
yā na yacchati durbuddhiḥ kāṣṭhīlā jāyate dhruvam  NarP 
tatpātakaviśuddhyarthaṃ dehi me dvādaśībhavam 
turīyāṃśamitaṃ puṇyaṃ yadyasti mayi te ghṛṇā  NarP 
etacchrutvā vacastasyāḥ kāṣṭhīlāyāḥ sulocane 
puṇyaṃ dattavatī tasyai pāṇau vāri pragṛhya ca  NarP 
yatkṛtaṃ hi mayā pūrvamekādaśyā mupoṣaṇam 
tatturīyāṃśapuṇyena kāṣṭhīleyaṃ vimucyatām  NarP 
pūrvajanmakṛtātpāpātsatyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam 
evamukte tu vacane mayā vidyutsamaprabhā  NarP 
dṛṣṭā divyavimānasthā gacchantī vaiṣṇavaṃ padam 
patirhi daivataṃ loke vañcanīyo na bhāryayā  NarP 
dehena cāpi vittena yadīcchecchobhanāṃ gatim 
sā tvaṃ brūhi pradāsyāmi bharturarthe tavepsitam  NarP 
vittaṃ dehaṃ tathā putraṃ yaccānyadvā varānane 
kimanyaddaivataṃ loke strīṇāmekaṃ patiṃ vinā  NarP 
tasyārthe vā tyajedvittaṃ jīvitaṃ vā sulocane 
kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate  NarP 
agnyādisākṣye vṛtamīkṣya niṣṭhurā yuktaṃ sudhorairvyasanairdvijātmajā 
patiṃ dadau naiva ca yācitā dhanaṃ tenaiva pāpena babhūva kīṭā  NarP 
etanmayā duṣṭamanaṅgayaṣṭi kaumārabhāve pitṛveśmavāse 
jñātvā hitaṃ tathyamidaṃ svabharturdadāmi sarvaṃ ca gṛhāṇa subhru  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite kāṣṭhīlopākhyāne māghamāhātmyaṃ nāmaikatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
vasiṣṭha uvāca
saṃdhyāvalīvacaḥ śrutvā mohinī duhitā vidheḥ 
uvāca tatparā svīye kārye mohakaraṇḍikā  NarP 
yadyevaṃ tvaṃ vijānāsi dharmādharmagatiṃ śubhe 
bharturarthe pradātrī ca dhanajīvitayorapi  NarP 
tadāhaṃ yācaye vittaṃ jīvitādadhikaṃ śubhe 
dehi putraśiroḥ mahyaṃ yadiṣṭaṃ hṛdayādhikam  NarP 
yadi no bhojanaṃ kuryātsaṃprāpte harivāsare 
tadā svahaste saṃgṛhya khaḍgaṃ rājā patistava  NarP 
dharmāṅgadaśiraścāru candrabiṃbopamaṃ śubham 
ajātaśmaśrukaṃ caiva kuṇḍalābhyāṃ vibhūṣitam  NarP 
chitvā śīghraṃ pātayatu mamotsaṃge sulocane 
etadvā kurutadbhadre yadānnaṃ na bhunakti ca  NarP 
dine mādhavadevasya pāpasaṃghavināśane 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasyā mohinyāḥ kaṭukākṣaram  NarP 
pracakaṃpe kṣaṇaṃ devī śītārtā kadalī yathā 
saṃdhyāvalī tato dhairyamāsthāya varavārṇinī  NarP 
uvāca mohinīṃ vākyaṃ sumukhī prahasaṃtyapi 
śrūyante hi purāṇeṣu gāthāḥ subhru samīritāḥ  NarP 
dvādaśī prati saṃbaddhāḥ svargamokṣapradāyikāḥ 
dhanaṃ tyajettyajeddārāñjīvitaṃ ca gṛhaṃ tyajet  NarP 
tyajeddeśaṃ tathā bhūpaṃ svargaṃ mitraṃ guruṃ tyajet 
tyajettīrthaṃ tyajeddharmaṃ tyajedatyantasupriyam  NarP 
tyajedyogaṃ tyajeddānaṃ jñānaṃ puṇyakriyā tyajet 
tapastyajettyajedvidyāṃ siddhiṃ mokṣaṃ tyajecchubhe  NarP 
na tyajeddvādagaśīṃ puṇyāṃ pakṣayorubhayorapi 
iha saṃbandhinaḥ sarve putrabhrātṛsuhṛtpriyāḥ  NarP 
aihikāmuṣmike devi sādhanī dvādaśī smṛtā 
dvādaśyāstu prabhāveṇa sarvaṃ kṣemaṃ bhaviṣyati  NarP 
dāpaye tava tuṣṭyarthaṃ dharmāṅgadaśiraḥ śubhe 
viśvāsaṃ kuru me vākye sukhinī bhava śobhane  NarP 
ihārthaṃ śrūyate bhadre itihāsaḥ purātanaḥ 
kathayiṣyāmi te bhadre sāvadhānā śruṇuṣva me  NarP 
āsīdvirocanaḥ pūrvaṃ daityo dharmaparāyaṇaḥ 
tasya bhāryā viśālākṣī dvijapūjanatatparā  NarP 
nityamekamṛṣiṃ prātaḥ pūjayitvā yathāvidhi 
pādodakaṃ tasya subhru bhaktyā pibati hṛṣṭadhīḥ  NarP 
prāhlādiśaṅkitā devā āsanpūrvaṃ mṛte sati 
hiraṇyakaśipau rājyaṃ śāsati hyugratejasi  NarP 
prāhlādau hlādasaṃyukte cerurvyagrā mahītale 
ekadā śakramukhyāste devāḥ samantrya vākpatim  NarP 
procuḥ kiṃ kāryamadhunāsmābhiḥ śatru pratāpitaiḥ 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ teṣāṃ devānāṃ gururabravīt  NarP 
viṣṇurvijñāpanīyo 'dya duḥkhaṃ prāptaiḥ suravrajaiḥ 
tacchrutvā bhāṣitaṃ tasya guroramitatejasaḥ  NarP 
virocanaprāṇahatyai jagmurvaikuṇṭhamantike 
tatra gatvā suraśreṣṭhaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ stavaiḥ  NarP 
devā ūcuḥ
namo devādhidevāya viṣṇave 'mitatejase 
bhaktavighnavināśāya vaikuṇṭhāya namo namaḥ  NarP 
haraye 'dbhutasiṃhāya vāmanāya mahātmane 
kroḍarūpāya matsyāya pralayābdhinivāsine  NarP 
kūrmāya mandaradhṛte bhārgavāyābdhiśāyine 
rāmāyākhilanāthāya viśveśāya ca sākṣiṇe  NarP 
dattātreyāya śuddhāya kapilāyārtihāriṇe 
yajñāya dhṛtadharmāya sanakādisvarūpiṇe  NarP 
dhruvasya varadātre ca pṛthave bhūrikarmaṇe 
ṛṣabhāya viśuddhāya hayaśīrṣabhṛtātmane  NarP 
haṃsāyāgamarūpāyāmṛtakumbhavidhāriṇe 
kṛṣṇāṃya vāsudevāya saṃkarṣaṇavapurdhṛte  NarP 
pradyumnāyāniruddhāya brahmaṇe śaṅkarāya ca 
kumārāya gaṇeśāya nandine bhṛṅgiṇe namaḥ  NarP 
gandhamādanavāsāya naranārāyaṇāya ca 
jagannāthāya nāthāya namo rāmeśvarāya ca  NarP 
dvārakāvāsine caiva tulasī vanavāsine 
namaḥ kamalanābhāya namaste paṅkajāṅghraye  NarP 
namaḥ kamalahastāya kamalākṣāya te namaḥ 
kamalāpratipālāya keśavāya namo namaḥ  NarP 
namo bhāskararūpāya śaśirūpadharāya ca 
lokapālasvarūpāya prajāpativapurdhṛte  NarP 
bhūtagrāmasvarūpāya jīvarūpāya tejase 
jayāya jayine netre niyamāya kriyātmane  NarP 
nirguṇāya nirīhāya nītijñāyākriyātmane 
buddhāya kalkirūpāya kṣetrajñāyākṣarāya ca  NarP 
govindāya jagadbhartre 'nantāyādyāya śārṅgiṇe 
śaṅkhine gadine caiva namaścakradharāya ca  NarP 
khaḍgine śūline caiva sarvaśastrāstraghātine 
śaraṇyāya vareṇyāya parāya paramātmane  NarP 
hṛṣīkeśāya viśvāya viśvarūpāya te namaḥ 
kālanābhāya kālāya śaśisūryyadṛśe namaḥ 
pūrṇāya parisevyāya parātparatarāya ca  NarP 
jagatkartre jagadbhartre jagaddhātreṃ'takāya ca 
mohine kṣobhine kāmarūpiṇe 'jāya sūriṇe  NarP 
bhagavaṃstava saṃprāptāḥ śaraṇaṃ daityatāpitāḥ 
tadvidhatsvākhilādhāra yathā hi sukhino vayam  NarP 
putramitrakalatrādisaṃyutā viharāmahe 
tacchrutvā stavanaṃ teṣāṃ vaikuṇṭhaḥ prītamānasaḥ  NarP 
pradadau darśanaṃ teṣāṃ daityasaṃ saṃtāpitātmanām 
te dṛṣṭvā devadeveśaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ snigdhamānasam  NarP 
virocanavadhāyāśu prārthayāmāsurādarāt 
tacchrutvā śakramukhyānāṃ kāryaṃ kāryavidāṃ varaḥ  NarP 
samāśvāsya surānprītyā visasarja mudānvitān 
gateṣu devavargeṣu sarvopāyavidāṃvaraḥ  NarP 
vṛddhabrāhmaṇarūpeṇa virocanagṛhaṃ yayau 
dvijapūjanakāle tu saṃprāptaḥ kāryasādhakaḥ  NarP 
taṃ tu dṛṣṭvā viśālākṣī brāhmaṇaṃ hṛṣṭamānasā 
apūrvaṃ bhaktibhāvena dadau satkṛtya cāsanam  NarP 
so 'naṅgīkṛtya taddattamāsanaṃ prāha tāṃ śubhe 
nāhaṃ samādade devi tvaddattaṃ paramāsanam  NarP 
śṛṇu me kāryamatulaṃ yadarthamahamāgataḥ 
yanme manogataṃ kāryaṃ tadvijñāya ca mānini  NarP 
yoṃ'gīkaroti tatpūjāṃ grahīṣyāmi varānane 
tacchrutvā vṛddhaviprasya vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradā  NarP 
māyayā mohitā viṣṇoḥ strītvāccāhātiharṣitā 
viśālākṣyuvāca
yatte manogataṃ vipra taddāsyāmi gṛhāṇame  NarP 
āsanaṃ pādasalilaṃ dehi me vāñchitārthadam 
ityuktaḥ sa dvijaḥ prāha na pratyemi striyā vacaḥ  NarP 
tava bhartā yadi vadettadā me pratyayo bhavet 
tadākarṇya dvijenoktaṃ virocanagṛheśvarī  NarP 
patimākārayāmāsa tatraiva dvijasannidhau 
sa prāpto dūtavākyena prāhlādirhṛṣṭamānasaḥ  NarP 
antaḥpuraṃ yatra bhāryā viśālākṣī samāsthitā 
tamāgataṃ samālokya patiṃ dharmaparāyaṇā  NarP 
utthāya natvā viprāgryamāsanaṃ punararpayat 
yadā tu jagṛhe naiva dattamāsanamādarāt  NarP 
rājānaṃ kathayāmāsa daityānāṃ patimātmanaḥ 
taddṛttāntamupājñāya daityarāṭ sa virocanaḥ  NarP 
bhāryāsnehena mugdhātmā tattadāṅgīcakāra ha 
aṅgīkṛte tu daityena tadvijñāya ca mānasam  NarP 
uvāca brāhmaṇo hṛṣṭaḥ svamāyurmama kalpaya 
tatastu daṃpatī tatra mugdhau svakṛtayā śucā  NarP 
muhūrtaṃ dhyānamāsthāya karau baddhocaturdvijam 
gṛhāṇa jīvitaṃ vipra dehi pādodakaṃ mama  NarP 
tvayoktaṃ vacanaṃ satyaṃ kurvaḥ prītimavāpnuhi 
tatastu vipraḥ protātmā tadaṅgīkṛtya cāsanam  NarP 
pādodakaṃ dadau tasyai bhaktyā prīto janārdanaḥ 
prakṣālya pādau viprasya viśālākṣī mudānvitā  NarP 
patyā saha dadhau mūrdhni apaḥ pādāvanejanīḥ 
tatastu sahasā subhru daṃpatī divyarūpiṇau  NarP 
vimānavaramāruhya jagmaturvaiṣṇavaṃ padam 
tataḥ prasanno bhagavān devaśalyaṃ vimocya saḥ  NarP 
yayau vaikuṇṭhabhavanaṃ sarvairdevagaṇaiḥ stutaḥ 
evaṃ mayāpi dātavyaṃ tava devi pratiśrutam  NarP 
na satyāccālaye devi patiṃ rukmāṅgadābhidham 
sattayameva manuṣyāṇāṃ gatidaṃ parikīrtitam  NarP 
satyācccutaṃ manuṣyaṃ hi śvapākādadhamaṃ viduḥ  NarP 
ityevamuktvā kanakāvadātā sā mohinīṃ paṅkajajanmajātām 
jagrāha bhartuścaraṇau sutāmnau raktāṅgulī pāṇiyugena subhrūḥ  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite saṃdhyāvalīkathanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
vasiṣṭha uvāca
saṃdhyāvalī tataḥ pādau bhartuḥ saṃgṛhya bhūpate 
uvāca vacanaṃ devī dharmāṃ gadavināśanam  NarP 
bahudhāpyanuśiṣṭeyaṃ mayā bhūpa yathā tvayā 
mohinyā moharūpāyā nānyatsaṃrocate 'dhunā  NarP 
bhojanaṃ vāsare viṣṇorvadhaṃ vā tanayasya vai 
dharmatyāgādvaraṃ nātha putrasya vinipātanam  NarP 
yādṛśī hi jananyāstu pīḍā bhavati bhūpate 
putrasyotpādane tīvrātādṛśī na bhavetpituḥ  NarP 
garbhasaṃdhāraṇe rājan khedaḥ sneho 'dhiko yathā 
māturbhavati bhūpāla tathā nahi bhavetpituḥ  NarP 
bījanirvāṣakaḥ proktaḥ pitā rājendra bhūtale 
jananī dhāriṇī kliṣṭā varddhane pālane 'dhikā  NarP 
pituḥ śataguṇaḥ sneho mātuḥ putre pravartate 
snehādhikyaṃ tu saṃprekṣya mātaraṃ mahatīṃ viduḥ  NarP 
sāhaṃ jātā gatasnehā paralokajigīṣayā 
putrasya nṛpaśārdūla satyavākyasya pālanāt  NarP 
vyāpādaya sutaṃ bhūpa snehaṃ tyaktvā sudūrataḥ 
mā satyalaṅghanaṃ kārṣīḥ śāpito 'si mayātmanā  NarP 
nikaṣeṣu hyaṣīkeśo bhaviṣyati phalapradaḥ 
yasmiṃścīrṇe rujā dehe nālpāpi nṛpa jāyate  NarP 
adharmānmānavo 'vaśyaṃ svargabhraṣṭo na saṃśayaḥ 
prāṇānādāya putraṃ vā sarvasvaṃ vā mahīpate  NarP 
yaścānuvartate daivaṃ sa pumān gīyate mahān 
tā āpado 'pi bhūpāla dhanyā yāḥ satyakārikāḥ  NarP 
sattayasaṃrakṣaṇārthatvānnṛṇāṃ syurmokṣadāyikāḥ 
kīrtisaṃstaraṇārthāya karttavyaṃ manujaiḥ sadā  NarP 
karma bhūpāla śāstroktaṃ snehadveṣavivarjitam 
tadalaṃ paritāpena satyaṃ pālaya bhūpate  NarP 
satyasya pālanādrājanviṣṇudehena yujyate 
devairutpāditā hyeṣā nikaṣā te vimohinī  NarP 
manye bhūpāla sā patnyā kṛtā tāṃ tvaṃ na budhyase 
putravya pādanāddevā bhaviṣyanti hyavāṅmukhāḥ  NarP 
teṣāṃ datvā padaṃ mūrdhni yāsyase paramaṃ padam 
viṣṇorudvahatāṃ bhaktiṃ devatāḥ paripanthinaḥ  NarP 
bhaviṣyatyandhatā loke tadeva prakaṭīkṛtam 
viruddhā vibudhā bhūpa seśvarāstava ceṣṭitaiḥ  NarP 
mokṣamārgaprabhettārastava niścayā lopakāḥ 
sa tvaṃ bhūpa dṛḍho bhūtvā ghātayasva sutaṃ priyam  NarP 
mohinyāḥ kuru vākyaṃ tu ātmanaḥ satyapālanāt  NarP 
lupte 'pi vākye bhavitā nṛpeśa pāpaṃ samaṃ brahmavadhena ghoram 
tantāsi loke śamanasya bhūpa yaśaḥpraṇo bhavitā dharāyām  NarP 
vasiṣṭha uvāca
bhāryāyā vacanaṃ śrutvā rājā rukmāṅgadastadā 
saṃdhyāvalīmuvācedaṃ mohinyāḥ sannidhau nṛpa  NarP 
putrahatyā mahāhatyā brahmahatyādhikā priye 
ghātayitvā sutaṃ loke kā gatirmme bhaviṣyati  NarP 
kva gato mandaraṃ śailaṃ kva prāptā mohinī mayā 
dharmāṅgadavināśāya devi kālapriyā tviyam  NarP 
dharmajñaṃ vinayopetaṃ prajārañjanakārakam 
aprajaṃ ca sutaṃ hatvā kā gatirme bhaviṣyāti  NarP 
kuputrasyāpi hananāddevi duḥkhaṃ bhavetpituḥ  NarP 
kiṃ punarddharmaśīlasya gurusevāvidhāyinaḥ 
jambūdvīpamidaṃ bhuktaṃ mayā tu varavarṇini  NarP 
dvīpāni sapta bhuktāni tanayena tavādhunā 
viṣṇoraṃśo varārohe piturapyadhiko bhavet  NarP 
purāṇeṣu varārohe kavibhiḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
yo 'yamatyadhikaḥ putro dharmāṅgada iti kṣitau  NarP 
mama vaṃśasya cārvaṅgi kiṃ punarmama mānadaḥ 
aho duḥkhamanuprāptaṃ putrādapyadhikaṃ mayā  NarP 
punareva varārohe brūhi tvaṃ vacanaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
mohinīṃ mohasaṃprāptāṃ mama duḥkhapradāyinīm  NarP 
evamuktvā tu nṛpatiḥ priyāṃ sandhyāvalīṃ tadā 
samīpamāgatya nṛpo mohinīkṣidamabravīt  NarP 
na bhokṣye vāsare viṣṇorna hiṃsye tanayaṃ śubhe 
ātmānaṃ dārayiṣyāmi devīṃ sandhyāvalīṃ tathā  NarP 
anyadvā dāruṇaṃ karma karomi tava śāsanāt 
duṣṭāgrahamimaṃ subhru parityaja sutaṃ prati  NarP 
kiṃ phalaṃ bhavitā tubhyaṃ hatvā dharmāṅgadaṃ sutam 
bhojayitvā dine viṣṇoḥ ko lābho bhavitā vada  NarP 
dāso 'smi tava bhṛtyo 'smi vaśago 'smi varānane 
anyaṃ yācasva subhage varaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  NarP 
raktāśokasamānābhyāṃ tava cārvaṅgisarvaśaḥ 
anyatprayojanaṃ kiñcitkarttāsmi vaśagastava  NarP 
prasādaṃ kuru me devi putrabhikṣāṃ prayaccha me 
durlabho guṇavānputro durlabho harivāsaraḥ  NarP 
durlabhaḥ jāhnavītoyaṃ durlabhā jananī kṣitau 
durlabhaṃ hi kule janma durlabhā vaṃśajā priyā  NarP 
durlabhaṃ kāñcanaṃ dānaṃ durlabhaṃ haripūjanam 
durlabhā vaiṣṇavī dīkṣā durlabhaḥ smṛtisaṃgrahaḥ  NarP 
durlabhaḥ śaukare vāso durlabhaṃ haricintanam 
durlabho jāgaro viṣṇordurlabhā hyātmasatkriyā  NarP 
durlabhā putrasaṃprāptirdurlabhaṃ pauṣkaraṃ jalam 
durlabhaḥ śiṣṭasaṃsargo durlabhā bhaktirucyate  NarP 
durlabhaṃ kapilādānaṃ durlabhaṃ nīlamokṣaṇam 
kṛtaṃ śrāddhaṃ trayodaśyāṃ durlabhaṃ varavarṇini  NarP 
durlabhā vasudhā cīrṇaṃ vrataṃ pātakanāśanam 
dhenustilamayī subhru durlabhā vipragāminī  NarP 
dhātrīsnānaṃ varārohe durlabho harivāsaraḥ 
durlabhaṃ parvakāle tu snānaṃ śītalavāriṇā  NarP 
māghamāse viśeṣeṇa pratyūṣasamaye śubhe 
yathāśāstroditaṃ karma taddevi bhuvi durlabham  NarP 
durlabhaṃ kuśalaṃ pathyaṃ durlabhaṃ cauṣadhaṃ tathā 
vyādhervighātakaraṇaṃ durlabhaṃ śāstramārgataḥ  NarP 
durlabhaṃ smaraṇaṃ viṣṇormaraṇe varavarṇini 
evaṃ vaco varārohe kuru me dharmarakṣakam  NarP 
kiṃ vadhenevai cārvaṅgi prasādaṃ kartumarhasi 
sevitā viṣayāḥ samyakkṛtaṃ rājyamakaṇṭakam  NarP 
mayā mūrghni padaṃ dattaṃ devagoviprarakṣiṇām 
adṛṣṭaviṣayaṃ putraṃ nāhaṃ hiṃsye kadācana  NarP 
svahasteneha cārvaṅgi kiṃ nu pāpamataḥ param 
mohinyuvāca
dharmāṅgado na me śatrurnāhaṃ hanmi sutaṃ tava  NarP 
pūrvameva mayā proktaṃ bhuṅkṣvatvaṃ harivāsare 
vasudhāṃ svecchayā rājaṃstvaṃ śādhi bahuvatsaram  NarP 
nāhaṃ vyāpādaye putramarthasiddhistu bhojane 
mama bhūmipate kāryaṃ na putranidhane tava  NarP 
yadi putraḥ priyo rājanbhujyatāṃ harivāsare 
kiṃ vilāpairmahīpāla etairddharmabahiṣkṛtaiḥ  NarP 
satyaṃ saṃrakṣa yatnena kuruṣva vacanaṃ mama 
evaṃ bruvāṇāṃ tāṃ rājanmohinīṃ tanumadhyamām  NarP 
dharmāṅgadaḥ pratyuvāca dṛṣṭvā natvāgrataḥ sthitaḥ 
etadeva gṛhāṇa tvaṃ mā śaṅkāṃ kuru bhāmini  NarP 
gṛhītvā nirmalaṃ khaṅgaṃ vinyasya nṛpateḥ puraḥ 
ātmānaṃ ca pratyuvāca satyadharmavyavasthitaḥ  NarP 
na vilaṃbaḥ pitaḥ kāryastvayā mama nipātane 
manmāturvacanaṃ satyaṃ kuru bhūpa pratiśrutam  NarP 
ātmā rakṣyo dhanairdārairathavāpi nijātmajaiḥ 
apatyaṃ dharmakāmārthaṃ śreyaskāmasya bhūpateḥ  NarP 
tvadarthe maraṇaṃ mahyamakṣayya gatidāyakam 
tavāpi nirmanā lokāḥ svavākyaparipālanāt  NarP 
parityajya paraṃ duḥkhaṃ putravyāpādanodbhavam 
dehatyāge mamāraṃbho naradehe bhaviṣyati  NarP 
sarvāmayavinirmukte śatakratusame vibho 
piturarthe hatā ye tu māturarthe hatāstathā  NarP 
gavārthe brāhyaṇārthe vā pramadārthe mahīpate 
bhūmyarthe pārthivārthe vā devatārthe tathaiva ca  NarP 
bālārthe vikalārthe ca yānti lokānsubhāsvarān 
tadalaṃ paritāpena jahi māṃ tvaṃ varāsinā  NarP 
satyaṃ pālaya rājendra mā bhuṅkṣva harivāsare 
dharmārthe tanayaṃ hanyādbhāryāṃ vāpi mahīpate  NarP 
śrūyate vedavākyeṣu putraṃ hanyānmakhasthitaḥ 
aśvameghe makhavare na doṣo jāyate nṛpa  NarP 
yadbravīti mahīpāla mohinī jananī mama 
tattvayā hyavicāreṇa karttavyaṃ vacanaṃ dhruvam  NarP 
prasīda rājendra kuruṣva vākyaṃ mayeritaṃ cātmavadhāya satyam 
vimocayethā nṛpate sughorādvākyānṛtānmohinihastayogāt  NarP 
vadhena te bhūmipate sutasya yaśaḥ prakāśaṃ gamayiṣyate ca 
yaśaḥ pkāśādbhavitā hi kīrtistathākṣayā tāta na saṃśayo 'tra  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite dharmāṅgadoktirnāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
vasiṣṭha uvāca
tatputravacanaṃ śrutvā rājā rukmāṅgadastadā 
saṃdhyāvalīmukhaṃ prekṣya prahṛṣṭakamalopamam  NarP 
mohinīvacanaṃ śṛṇvanbhuṅkṣva mā hana dehajam 
mā bhuṅkṣva tanayaṃ hiṃsa cetyāgrahasamanvitam  NarP 
etasminneva kāle tu bhagavānkamalekṣaṇaḥ 
antarddhānagatastasthau vyomni dhairyāvalokakaḥ  NarP 
trayāṇāṃ nṛpaśārdūla meghaśyāmo nirañjanaḥ 
dharmāṅgadasya vīrasya tasya rukmāṅgadasya tu  NarP 
saṃdhyāvalyā sametasya vīśasaṃstho janārdanaḥ 
vacane bhuṅkṣva bhuṅkṣveti mohinyā vyāhṛte tadā  NarP 
jagrāha vimalaṃ khaṅgaṃ hantuṃ dharmāṅgadaṃ sutam 
supraharṣeṇa manasā praṇamya garuḍadhvajam 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā khaṅgahastaṃ tu pitaraṃ dharmmaṃbhūṣaṇaḥ  NarP 
praṇamya mātāpitarau devaṃ cakradharaṃ tathā 
vadanaṃ prekṣya cādīnaṃ jananyā nṛpapuṅgavaḥ  NarP 
vṛṣāṅgadena tu tadā svagrīvorvītale kṛtā 
kaṃbugrīvāṃ samānāṃ tu suvarṇā sukomalām  NarP 
bahurekhamatha sthūlāṃ khaṅgamārge jyadarśayat 
pitṛbhaktyā yutenaiva mātṛbhaktyādhikena vai  NarP 
grīvāpradāne tanayasya bhūpa harṣākule cārusudhāṃśuvaktre 
gṛhītakhaṅge jagadīśanāthe cacāla pṛthvīṃ sanagā samagrā  NarP 
siṃdhuḥ pravṛddhaśca babhūva sadyo nimajja nārthaṃ bhuvanatrayasya 
nipeturulkāḥ śataśo dharāyāṃ nirghātayuktāḥ sataḍitkhamadhyāt  NarP 
vivarṇarūpā ca babhūva mohinī na devakāryaṃ hi kṛtaṃ mayeti 
nirarthakaṃ janma mamādhunābhūtkṛtaṃ tu daivena dajagadvidhāyinā  NarP 
vimohanaṃ rūpamidaṃ viḍaṃbanaṃ yadbhūmipālena na bhuktamannam 
harerdine pāpabhayāpahe tu tṛṇaiḥ samāhaṃ bhavitā triviṣṭape  NarP 
satvādhiko yāsyati mokṣamārgaṃ gantāsmi pāpa narakaṃ sudāruṇam  NarP 
samudyate tadā khaṅge nṛpeṇa nṛpapuṅgava 
mohinī mohasaṃyuktā papāta dharaṇītale  NarP 
rājāpi tena khaṅgena bhrājamānaḥ samudyataḥ 
grīvāyāśchedanārthāya vṛṣāṅgadasutasya tu  NarP 
sakuṇḍalaṃ cāru śaśiprakāśaṃ bhrājiṣṇu vaktraṃ tanayasya bhūpaḥ 
pracicchide yāvadatīva harṣāddhairyānvito rukmavibhūṣaṇo 'sau  NarP 
tāvadgṛhītaḥ svakareṇa bhūpaḥ kṣīrābdhikanyāpatinā mahīpaḥ 
tuṣṭo 'smi tuṣṭo 'smi na saṃśayo 'tra gacchasva lokaṃ mama lokanātha  NarP 
priyānvitaścātmajasaṃyutaśca kīrtiṃ samādhāya mahītale tu 
trailokyapūjyāṃ vimalāṃ ca śuklāṃ kṛtvā padaṃ mūrdhni yamasya bhūpa  NarP 
prayāhi vāsaṃ mama dehasaṃjñaṃ sa cakriṇo bhūmipatiḥ kareṇa 
saṃspṛṣṭamātro virajā babhūva priyāsametastanayena yuktaḥ  NarP 
upetya vegena jagāma dehaṃ devasya divyaṃ sa nṛpo mahātmā 
vihāya lakṣmīmavanīprasūtāṃ vihāya dāsīḥsudhanaṃ sa kośam  NarP 
vihāya nāgāṃsturagānrathāṃśca svadāravargaṃ svajanādikāṃśca 
jagāma dehaṃ madhusūdanasya tatoṃ'barātpuṣpacayaḥ papāta  NarP 
saṃhṛṣṭasiddhaiḥ suralokapālaiḥ saṃtāḍitā dundubhayo vineduḥ 
rājan jagurgītamatīva ramyaṃ devāṅganāḥ saṃnanṛturmudānvitāḥ  NarP 
gandharvakanyā nṛpakarmatuṣṭāstadadbhutaṃ prekṣya dineśasūnuḥ 
harestanau bhūmipatiṃ praviṣṭaṃ sadāraputraṃ svalipiṃ pramārjya  NarP 
lokāṃśca sarvānnṛpadiṣṭamārge kṛtvā kṛtajñānharilokamārgān 
bhītaḥ punaḥ prāpya pitāmahāntikaṃ provāca devaṃ caturānanaṃ rudan  NarP 
nāhaṃ niyogī bhavitā hi deva ājñāvihīnaḥ suralokanātha 
vidhehi cānyatprakaromi tāta nideśanaṃ māstu madīya daṇḍam  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite sutavadhodyatasya rukmāṅgadasya bhagavaddarśanaṃ nāma catustriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
yama uvāca
vibudheśa jagannātha carācaraguro prabho 
mohinī niṣphalā jātā vandhyā strī janane yathā  NarP 
rukmāṅgadapraṇītena mārgeṇa kuśalāñchana 
lokaḥ prayāti vaikuṃṇṭhaṃ na māṃ kaścitprapadyate  NarP 
gate 'pi bhūminātheśe dehaṃ devasya cakriṇaḥ 
tathāpi sarvabhūtānāṃ na buddhiḥ parivartate  NarP 
upoṣya vāsaraṃ viṣṇorākumārāttu mānavāḥ 
prayānti paramaṃ lokaṃ luptapāpāḥ pitāmaha  NarP 
putrī te vrīḍitā devī mohinī mohamāgatā 
nāyāti tava sāmīpyaṃ na bhuṅkte lokagarhitā  NarP 
nirvyāpārastvahaṃ jātaḥ kiṃ karomi praśādhi mām 
raviputravacaḥ śrutvā provāca kamalāsanaḥ  NarP 
gacchāmaḥ sahitāḥ sarve mohinīṃ pratibodhitum 
mohinyāṃ pratibuddhāyāṃ kariṣyāmo divākare  NarP 
tava kāryaṃ na saṃdehaḥ saṃbhramastyajyatāmayam 
tato deva gaṇāḥ sarve śatakratupurogamāḥ  NarP 
brahmaṇā sahitāḥ pṛthvīṃ vimānaiḥ sūryasaprabhaiḥ 
samāyātā mahīpāla nārīṃ tāṃ pratibodhitum  NarP 
te vimānaiḥ samantāttu parivārya śubhānanām 
tejohīnāṃ nirānandāṃ śuṣkatoyāṃ nadīmiva  NarP 
śaśihīnāṃ niśāṃ bhūpa ṛtvigghīnāṃ kriyāmiva 
parājito yathā martyaḥ pralmānakusumaṃ yathā  NarP 
nivṛttotsavavedīva vidrumaṃ dhavalaṃ yathā 
gataśālistu kedāro niṣpra yathā  NarP 
maṇḍa vā gatodvā yathā saraḥ 
manthānaṃ navanīte vā uddhṛte dharaṇīpate  NarP 
asaṃskṛtā yathā vāṇī marditā ca yathā camūm 
hata nāthāṃ tu yuvatīṃ dhānyahīnāṃ prajāṃ yathā  NarP 
mantrahīnavidhiṃ yuddhaṃ dharmaṃ ca dayayā vinā 
pṛthvīṃ bhūpālahīnā vā mantrahī yathā nṛpa  NarP 
dhanadhānyavihīnaṃ vā gṛhaṃ nṛpavarottama 
jalahīnaṃ yathā kuṃbhaṃ paṅkasthaṃ gopatiṃ yathā  NarP 
gṛhasthaṃ bhāryayā hīnaṃ rāṣṭrabhraṣṭaṃ ca bhūpatim 
bhagnakriyaṃ yathā vaidyaṃ bhagnaśākhaṃ yathā drumam  NarP 
tejohīnaṃ yathāgāraṃ nirjalaṃ vā ghanaṃ yathā 
vidhūma iva saptārcirviraśmiriva bhāskaraḥ  NarP 
matibhraṣṭo yathā martyaḥ parvasaṃgī yathā naraḥ 
atṛptaḥ kāntayā kāntaḥ pannagaśca viṣojjhitaḥ  NarP 
lūnapakṣo yathā pakṣī vṛttihīno yathā dvijaḥ 
śirobhraṣṭā yathā mālā parvato dhātuvarjitaḥ  NarP 
prabhraṣṭalipi śāstraṃ vā ṛgyajurvisvaraṃ yathā 
svarahīnaṃ yathā sāma padmahīnaṃ yathā saraḥ  NarP 
yathā mārgaṃ tṛṇai ruddhaṃ padmaṃ patravivarjitam 
jñānaṃ mamatvasaṃyuktaṃ pumāṃsaṃ prakṛtiṃ vinā  NarP 
sāṃkhyāni tattvahīnāni dharmaṃ daṃbhānvitaṃ yathā 
tejohīnāṃ tathāpaśyan mohinīṃ te divaukasaḥ  NarP 
dhyāyamānāṃ nirutsāhāṃ dṛśyamānāṃ janaiḥ prabho 
ākrośavacanaiḥ krūraiḥ putrahatyāsamanvitām  NarP 
duḥśīlāṃ dharmasaṃtyaktāṃ tadvākyaparimoṣitām 
svavākyapālanāṃ caṇḍāmucurdevāḥ samāgatāḥ  NarP 
māṃ śokaṃ kuru vāmoru pauruṣaṃ hi tvayā kṛtam 
nahi mādhavabhaktānāṃ vidyate mānakhaṇḍanam  NarP 
sā tvaṃ hariṇaśāvākṣi devakāryārthamāgatā 
tanna siddhaṃ varārohe sa prayāto 'dhunābhavam  NarP 
vighnavidhvaṃsinīṃ pūrvaṃ kṛtā rukmāṅgadena hi 
ekādaśī mahāpuṇyā mohinī mādhave site  NarP 
saṃvatsaraṃ viśālākṣi kṛcchrapādaprapūjitā 
tasyaivādhyuṣṭiratulā yatsatyācaccalito na hi  NarP 
vighnarājñī tu vai nārī lokeṣu parigīyate 
karmaṇā manasā vācā putravyāpādane matim  NarP 
kṛtvā coddhṛtya khaṅgaṃ ca tyaktvā snehaṃ sudūrurataḥ 
tādṛśaṃ nikaṣaṃ prokṣya bhagavānmadhusūdanaḥ  NarP 
haniṣyati priyaṃ putraṃ na bhuṅkte harivāsare 
putrasya ca priyāyāśca bhāvaṃ prekṣya nṛpasya ca  NarP 
viṣṇunā paretuṣṭena nītāḥ svabhavane trayaḥ 
sadehāḥ kṣīṇakarmāṇo hy aṅgāro 'gnirivāhitaḥ  NarP 
phalaṃ karmaṇi cārabdhe yadi devī na siddhyati 
sarvayatnena subhage doṣaḥ ko 'tra tavādhunā  NarP 
etasmād varadāḥ sarve saṃprāptā vibudhāḥ śubhe 
siddhau vāpyatha vāsiddhau karmakṛtsyāddṛthā na hi  NarP 
bhartavyo bhṛtyavargaśca bhūbhujā dharmamicchatā 
sadbhāve ghaṭamānasya yadi karma na siddhyati  NarP 
deyaṃ vetanamātraṃ tu na ca tuṣṭiphalaṃ bhavet 
yo na tasmai prayaccheta jīvanaṃ jīvanāya vai  NarP 
govadhaṃ samavāpnoti sa naro nātra saṃśayaḥ 
tasmād deyaṃ varārohe abhīṣṭaṃ varasundari  NarP 
sadbhāvena kṛte samyagvighnaṃ kāryaṃ divaukasām 
kiṃ na kurvanti vibudhās tvayā saha varānane  NarP 
dvādaśyās tejasā bhagnā yām āhur vighranāśinīm 
vibudhair evam uktā tu mohinī lokamohinī  NarP 
uvāca sā nirānandā patihīnātiduḥkhitā 
dhigidaṃ jīvitaṃ mahyaṃ yena kāryaṃ na sādhitam  NarP 
na kṛto janasaṃbādho yamamārgo 'marādhipāḥ 
na tu luptaṃ haridinaṃ na bhuktaṃ harivāsare  NarP 
bhūbhujā tena vīreṇa kṛtaḥ putravadho mudā 
gato mūrdhni padaṃ datvā mama rukmāṅgado harim  NarP 
aprameyaguṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirmalaṃ nirmalāśrayam 
haṃsaṃ śucipadaṃ vyoma praṇavaṃ bījamavyayam  NarP 
nirākāraṃ nirābhāsaṃ niṣprapañcaṃ nirañjanam 
śūnyaṃ viyatsvarūpaṃ ca dhyeyadhyānavivarjitam  NarP 
asti nāstīti yaṃ prāhurna dūre nāpi cāntike 
paraṃ dhāma manogrāhyaṃ puruṣākhyaṃ jaganmayam  NarP 
hṛtpaṅkajasamāsīnaṃ tejorūpaṃ sanātanam 
tasmiṃl layam anuprāpte kiṃ nu me jīvite phalam  NarP 
asādhite tu yaḥ kārye naro gṛhṇāti vetanam 
svāminaṃ tu parityajya prayāti narakaṃ dhruvam  NarP 
na sādhayanti ye kāryaṃ svāmināṃ tu divaukasaḥ 
bhṛtyā vetanabhoktāro jāyante bhūtale hayāḥ  NarP 
asādhinīyaṃ kāryasya bhartṛputravināśinī 
kathaṃ varaṃ tu gṛhṇāmi bhavatāṃ nākavāsinām  NarP 
devā ūcuḥ
brūhi mohini dāsyāmi yatte hṛdi samīhitam 
anṛṇāstu bhaviṣyāmaḥ kṛtvā copakṛtiṃ tava  NarP 
pariśramaḥ kṛto devi tvayā rājaprayojane 
tasya tvaṃ phalabhāgdevi tādṛśārthe kṛtasya tu  NarP 
evamuccaramāṇānāṃ devatānāṃ mahīpate 
nṛpaterājagāmātha purodhāḥ pāvakaprabhaḥ  NarP 
uṣito jalamadhye tu prāṇāyāmarato muniḥ 
dvādaśābde tataḥ pūrṇe nirgato jalamadhyataḥ  NarP 
nirgatena śrutaṃ tena mohinīceṣṭitaṃ nṛpa 
sakrodho muniśārdūlo devavṛndamupāgataḥ  NarP 
uvāca vibudhānsarvānmohinīvaradāyinaḥ 
dhigimāṃ dhigdevasaṃghaṃ karma dhikpāpasaṃjñitam  NarP 
bhavatāṃ bhāvanāśāya puruṣārthe prarohakam 
bhavanto yacca dātāro mohinyā vāñchitaṃ varam  NarP 
hatyāyutā bhartṛsutopaghātinī vihinavṛttiśca marāśirūpā 
nāsmā hi loke bhavatīha śuddhiḥ samiddhavahnau patane 'pi devāḥ  NarP 
hatyāyutaṃ bhartṛvadho nirarthakametatsamaṃ vipravaraiḥ purākṛtam 
na cāpi cāsyā bhavatīha śuddhiḥ samidbhavahnau patane 'pi devāḥ  NarP 
vimoyitvā vacanaiḥ sudhāmayairukmāṅgadaṃ dharmaṃvibhūṣaṇaṃ ca 
priyāyutaṃ mokṣapadaṃ nihatya cakāra bhūmiṃ nṛpavarjitāṃ ca  NarP 
na cāpi vāso narakeṣu devā asyāḥ sthitiḥ kka tridive 'lpabuddheḥ 
na cāpi rājño nikaṭe ca devā nāpyetu viṣṇoḥ padamavyayaṃ yat  NarP 
na lokavādena vidūṣitāyā lokeṣu kutrāpi bhavecca vāsaḥ 
dhirajīvanaṃ kargmavigarhitāyā devāḥ sadā pāpasamāratāyāḥ  NarP 
patiṃ hatvā sutaṃ hatvā sapatnīṃ jananīsamām 
hatvā dharāṃ samastāṃ vā kāṃ gatiṃ yāsyate surāḥ  NarP 
iyaṃ pāpatarā devā dharmavidhvaṃsinī hareḥ 
sarvadāpyanayā proktaṃ bhujyatāṃ harivāsare  NarP 
prāṇasaṃvarddhanārthāya teṣāmevāpyadhogatiḥ 
bhujyatāṃ vāsare viṣṇorhanyatāṃ gaurdvijānvitā  NarP 
apeyaṃ pīyatā muktvā kathaṃ vāsaṃ labheddivi 
etadajñānināṃ proktaṃ jñānanāṃ tu na nirṇayaḥ  NarP 
ajñānāvdyāhṛte vākye bhujyatāṃ harivāsare 
tasyāpi śuddhirgaditā prāṇāyāmaśatena hi  NarP 
athavāpyupavāsena ekādaśyā divaukasaḥ 
ṛkṣeṇa saṃyutāyāstu jyeṣṭhakuṇḍāplavena vā  NarP 
śaukarasparśanā dvāpi naro devārcanena vā 
vyāhṛte kathitaṃ vipraiḥ seyamadya suniṣṭhurā  NarP 
bhojane pāpaniratā dine viṣṇordurāsade 
bharturvākyaṃ vyapohyaiva ghātayitvā sutaṃ priyam  NarP 
vākyajñaṃ vākyanirataṃ mātṝṇāṃ tu hite ratam 
viṣṇudharmapraloptrīyaṃ bahupāpasamanvitā  NarP 
naiṣā spṛśyāsti deveśāḥ kathamasyā varapradāḥ 
bhavanto nyāyayukteṣu dharmayukteṣu tatparāḥ  NarP 
pālanaṃ pāpayuktasya na kurvanti divaukasaḥ 
dharmādhārāḥ smṛtā devā dharmo vedesamāsthitaḥ  NarP 
vedaiḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ bhartuḥ strīṇāṃ dharmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
yadbravīti patiḥ kiñcittatkāryamāviśaṅkayā  NarP 
śuklaṃ śuklamiti brūyātkṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇeti cāmarāḥ 
śuśrūṣā sā hi vijñeyā na śuśrūṣā hi sevanam  NarP 
bharturājñā hatā devā ātmājñāsthāpanecchayā 
tasmātpāpā na saṃdeho mohinī sarvayoṣitām 
satyasya sādhanārthāya śapathairyantrito nṛpaḥ  NarP 
uvāca vividhaṃ vākyaṃ sā naicchatputraghātinī 
tena mokṣaṃ gato rājā pāpamasyāṃ visṛjya ca  NarP 
seyaṃ pāpaśarīrā hi hatyāyutasamanvitā  NarP 
dātāraṃ sarvadānānāṃ brahmaṇyaṃ haridaivatam 
prajārañjanaśīlaṃ ca harivāsarasevinam  NarP 
paradāreṣu niḥsnehaṃ viṣaye vigataspṛham 
parārthatyaktakāmaṃ ca sadā makhaniṣeviṇam  NarP 
sadaiva duṣṭadamane vartamānaṃ dharātale 
vyasanaiḥ saptabhirghorairanākrāntaṃ mahīpatim  NarP 
saṃnirasya durācārā varayogyā kathaṃ bhavet 
yo 'syāḥ pakṣetu varteta devo vā dānavo 'pi vā  NarP 
taṃ cāpi bhasmasātkuryāṃ kṣaṇena surasattamāḥ 
mohinyā rakṣaṇe yastu prayatnaṃ kurute surāḥ  NarP 
tasya tajjāyate pāpaṃ yanmohinyāṃ vyavasthitam  NarP 
sa evamuktvā nṛpate dvijendraḥ saṃgṛhya pāṇau salilaṃ ca tīvram 
krodhena saṃvīkṣya vidhiprasūtāṃ cikṣepa tanmūrghnyanalaprakāśam  NarP 
nikṣiptamātre salile mahīpa sadyaḥ prajajvāla ca taccharīram 
saṃpaśyatāṃ nākanivāsināṃ tu tṛṇyā yathā vahniśikhāvalīḍhā  NarP 
kopaṃ vibho saṃhara saṃhareti yāvadgiraḥ khe marutāṃ babhūvuḥ 
tāvatsa vahnirdvijavākyamṛṣṭo bhasmāvaśeṣāṃ pramadāṃ cakāra  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinī carite śāpaprāptirnāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
vasiṣṭha uvāca
mohinī mohamutsṛjya gatā vibudhamandiram 
bhartsitā devadūtena sthitiste 'tra na pāpinī  NarP 
pāpaśīle sudurmedhe bhartṛnindāparāyaṇe 
harivāsaralopinyāṃ vāsaste na triviṣṭape  NarP 
dharmato vimukhānāṃ ca narake vāsa iṣyate 
evamuktvā tu tāṃ vāyuḥ krūraṃ vacanapadbhutam  NarP 
tāḍayitvā ca daṇḍena prerayāmāsa yātanām 
evaṃ saṃtāḍitā rājan devadūtena mohinī  NarP 
brahmadaṇḍaparābhūtā saṃprāptā narakaṃ nṛpa 
tatra dharmājñayā sā tu dūtaiḥ saṃtāḍitā ciram  NarP 
sarveṣu kramaśo gatvā narakeṣu nipātitā 
pāpe dharmāṅgadaḥ putro ghātitaḥ patipāṇinā  NarP 
tvayā yatastato bhuṅkṣva kṛtakarmaphalaṃ tviha 
prajāhitaṃ sthiraprajñaṃ mahendravaruṇopamam  NarP 
saptadvīpādhipaṃ putraṃ hatvedṛkphalabhoginī 
prākṛtasyāpi putrasya hiṃsāyāṃ brahmahā bhavet  NarP 
kiṃ punarddharmayuktasya pāpe dharmāṅgadasya ca 
evaṃ nirbhatsitā dūtairyamasya nṛpasattama  NarP 
bubhuje yātanāḥ sarvāḥ kramaśaḥ śamanoditāḥ 
brahmadaṇḍahatāyāstu dehasparśena yātanāḥ  NarP 
jvalitāṅgā babhūvustā dhāraṇāya na tu kṣamāḥ 
tataste narakā rājan dharmarājamupāgatāḥ  NarP 
procuḥ prāñjalayo bhītāstadaṅgasparśapīḍitāḥ 
devadeva jagannātha dharmarāja dayāṃ kuru  NarP 
imāṃ niḥsārayāśu tvaṃ yātanābhyaḥ sukhāya naḥ 
yasyāḥ sparśanato nātha bhasmabhūtāḥ kṣaṇādaho  NarP 
bhaviṣyāmastatastvenāṃ narakebhyo vivāsaya 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ teṣāṃ dharmarājo 'tivismitaḥ  NarP 
dūtānsvānpratyuvāceyaṃ niḥsāryā mama mandirāt 
yo brahmadaṇḍanirdagdhaḥ pumān strī vā ca taskaraḥ  NarP 
tasya pāpasya saṃsparśaṃ necchati yātanā mama 
tasmādimāṃ mahāpāpāṃ bharturvacanalopinīm  NarP 
putraghnīṃ dharmahantrīṃ ca brahmadaṇḍahatāmapi 
niḥsārayata me bāpi deho jvalati darśaṃnāt  NarP 
ityuktāste tadā dūtā dharmarājena bhūpate 
praharanto 'straśastraiśca bahiścakruryamakṣayāt  NarP 
tataḥ sā duḥkhitā rājan mohinī mohasaṃyutā 
pātālaṃ prayayau tatra pātālasthairnivāritā  NarP 
tatastu vrīḍitātyarthaḥ mohinī brahmaṇaḥ sutā 
janakasyāntikaṃ gatvā duḥkhaṃ svaṃ saṃnyavedayat  NarP 
tāta tannāsti me sthānaṃ trailokye sacarā care 
yatra yatra tu gacchāmi tatra tatra kṣipanti mām  NarP 
ahaṃ nirvāsitā lokairghātayitvāyudhairdṛḍham 
bhavadājñāṃ samādāya gatā rukmavibhūṣaṇam  NarP 
mayā vyavasitaṃ cedaṃ sarvalokavigarhitam 
kleśayitvā tu bhartāraṃ putraṃ hatvā varāsinā  NarP 
saṃdhyāvalīṃ kṣobhayitvā pitaḥ prāptā daśā mimām 
na gatirvidyate deva pāpāyā mama sāṃpratam  NarP 
viśeṣāddvijaśāpena jātāhaṃ duḥkhabhāginī 
vipravākyahatānā ca dagdhānāṃ citrabhānunā  NarP 
divākīrtihatānāṃ ca bhakṣitānāṃ mṛgādibhiḥ 
śatahradāvipannānāṃ muktidā svarṇadī pitaḥ  NarP 
yadi tvaṃ tridaśaiḥ sārddhaṃ vipraṃ taṃ śāpadāyinam 
prasādayasi matprītyā tarhi me vihitā gatiḥ  NarP 
tāṃ tathāvādinīṃ rājan brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
śivendradharmasūryāgnideveśairmunibhiryutaḥ  NarP 
mohinīmagrataḥ kṛtvā jagāma dvijasannidhau 
tatra gatvā mahīpāla brahmā devādibhirvṛtaḥ  NarP 
mahatā gauraveṇāpi namaścakre svayaṃ vidhiḥ 
bhūpa rudrādidevaistu pūjyo mānyaḥ pitāmahaḥ  NarP 
mohinīprītaye mugdhaḥ svayaṃ cakre namaskriyām 
kārye mahati saṃprāpte hyasādhye bhuvanatraye  NarP 
na dūṣitaṃ bhavedbhūpa yaviṣṭhasyābhivādanam 
sa dvijo vedavedāṅgaparagastapasi sthitaḥ  NarP 
saṃprekṣya lokakartāraṃ devaiḥ saha samāgatam 
samutthāya namaścakre brahmāṇaṃ tānmunīnsurān  NarP 
vāsayāmāsa bhaktyā ca stutiṃ cakre 'bjajanmanaḥ 
tataḥ prasanno bhagavān lokakarttā jagadguruḥ  NarP 
te dvijaṃ prārthayāmāsurmohinyarthe nṛpārcitam 
tāta vipra sadācāra paralokopakāraka  NarP 
kṛpāṃ kuru kṛpāsiṃdho mohinīgatido bhava 
mayā saṃpreṣitā brahman rukmāṅgadavimohane  NarP 
sutā me yamalokaṃ tu śūnyaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca mānada 
vaikuṇṭhaṃ saṃkulaṃ prekṣya lokaiḥ sarvairni rākulaiḥ  NarP 
manasotpāditā devī devānāṃ hitakāriṇī 
niśāmaya dharādeva yadbravīmi tavāgrataḥ  NarP 
gatiṃ dharmasyātisūkṣmāṃ lokakalyāṇakāriṇīm 
anayā nikaṣāśyāṅgyā parīkṣya svarṇabhūṣaṇaḥ  NarP 
sadāraḥ sasuto brahmanprāpito harimandiram 
rājñāprahatayā bhaktyā harivāsarapālanāt  NarP 
kṛtaṃ śūnyaṃ yamasthānaṃ lipimārjanakarmaṇā 
devāpakāro viprarṣe na kṣamo bāhujanmanā  NarP 
bhūsurāṇāṃ viśeṣeṇaṃ yātāste tatsahāyakāḥ  NarP 
na prāpyate sāṅghyavidā tu yacca nāṣṭāṅgayogena tu bhaktigamyam 
tatprāpitaṃ bhūsura bhūpabharturnijasya putrasya tathā sapatnyāḥ  NarP 
yatpuṇyaśīlasya nṛpasya bhūpaśiromaṇerācaritaṃ pratīpam

devārthameṣā bhavavarddhanārthaṃ nṛpopakārāya ca saṃpravṛttā

dayāṃ kuruṣva praśamaṃ bhajasva piṣṭasya peṣo nahi nītiyuktaḥ 
śāpapradānenanipātiteyaṃ kuru prasādaṃ gatido bhavatvam 
yasminkṛte brāhmaṇa mohinīyaṃ buddhiṃ tyajetkrūratarāṃ tvayījye  NarP 
sa evamuktaḥ kamalāsanena vimṛśya buddhyā visasarja kopam

bahupāpayutā deva mohinī tanayā tava 
na lokeṣu sthitistasmātprāṇibhiḥ saṃkuleṣu ca  NarP 
mayā vimṛśya suciraṃ moddinyarthaṃ vicintitam 
taddāsyami tava prītyā tvaṃ hi pūjyataro mama  NarP 
yathā tava vacaḥ satyaṃ mama cāpi sureśvara 
devakāryaṃ ca bhavitā mohinīkṛtatyameva ca  NarP 
yannākrāntaṃ hi bhūtaughaistatsthāne mohinīsthitiḥ 
jaṅgamājaṅgamairbhūmirvyāptā dvīpavatī sadā  NarP 
talāni cāpi daityādyairākāśaḥ pakṣipūrvakaiḥ 
nākaḥ sukṛtibhirjīvairnarakāḥ pāpakarmabhiḥ  NarP 
jhaṣādyaiḥ sāgarā vyāptā naiṣvaspṛṣyāsthitistataḥ 
tato brahmā suraiḥ sarvaiḥ saṃmantrya nṛpasattama  NarP 
uvāca mohinīṃ devīṃ nāsti sthānaṃ tava kvacit 
tacchrutvā mohinī vākyaṃ piturājñāvidhāyinī  NarP 
uvāca praṇatā sarvān harivāsaranāśinī 
purodhasā sametāno devānāṃ lokasākṣiṇām  NarP 
bhavatāṃ tridaśaśreṣṭhā eṣa baddho mayāñjaliḥ 
praṇipātaśatenāpi prasannena hṛdā surāḥ  NarP 
dātavyaṃ yācitaṃ maṃhyaṃ sarveṣāṃ prītikārakam 
ekādaśyāḥ prabhāveṇa sarveṣāṃ pāpināṃ gatiḥ  NarP 
sādhyate tāṃ suraśreṣṭhā vardhituṃ me prayojanam 
patiḥ sapatnī putraśca mayā vaikuṇṭhagāḥ kṛtāḥ  NarP 
bhūrloke vidhavādyāhaṃ vartāmi bhavatāṃ kṛte 
yathā haridinaṃ duṣṭaṃ jāyate mama mānadāḥ  NarP 
etatprayāce dadata svārthārthaṃ taddhi nānyathā  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite ṣaṭtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mohinyuvāca
ekādaśīsamaṃ devāḥ pāvanaṃ nāparaṃ bhavet 
yayā pūtā mahāpāpā gacchanti harimandiram  NarP 
tatsamīpe mama sthānaṃ yuktaṃ bhāti vicāryatām 
devā ūcuḥ
vedho niśīthe devānāmupakārāya mohinī  NarP 
sūryodaye surāṇāṃ ca hariṇā parikalpitaḥ 
pāraṇaṃ ca trayodaśyāmupavāsavināśanam  NarP 
mahādvādaśikā hyaṣṭau yāḥ smṛtā vaiṣṇavāgame 
tāstu hyekādaśībhinnā upoṣyante ca vaiṣṇavaiḥ  NarP 
ekādaśīvrataṃ bhinnaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām 
nityaṃ pakṣadvaye proktaṃ vidhinā tridinātmake  NarP 
sāyaṃ prātastyajedbhuktiṃ kramātpūrvāparāhṇayoḥ 
ekādaśī yadā bhinnā upoṣyā hi pare 'hani 
dvādaśyāṃ hi vrataṃ kāryaṃ niraṃbu samupoṣaṇam  NarP 
laṅghane tvasamarthānāṃ jalaṃ śākaṃ phalaṃ payaḥ 
naivedyaṃ vā hareḥ proktaṃ svāhārātpādasaṃmitam  NarP 
svātī sūryodaye viddho tyajantyakādaśīṃ sati 
niṣkāmā madhyarātre ca viddhāṃ muñcanti yāmyayā  NarP 
sarveṣvapi tu lokeṣu viditā daśamī tithiḥ 
yamasya tasyāḥ prānti tu sthitiḥ kāryā tvayānaghe  NarP 
etena devakāryaṃ ca siddhaṃ bhavati śobhane 
sūryenducārā tithyāstu daśamyāḥ prāntagāminī  NarP 
bhuvi tīrthāni caiva tvaṃ svāghanāśāya saṃcara 
aruṇodayamārabhya yāvatsūryodayo bhavet  NarP 
tadantastvaṃ vrate prāptā labhasvaikādaśīphalam 
yaḥ kaścitkurute viddhaṃ tvayā hyekādaśīvratam  NarP 
sa tīpakārakastubhyaṃ bhaviṣyati surapriye 
muhūrtadvayamātraṃ tu jñeyaṃ cātrāruṇodayam  NarP 
mūhūrtāḥ pañcadaśa ca smṛtā rātrerdinasya ca 
jñeyāste hrasvadīrghatve trairāśika vidhānataḥ  NarP 
trayodaśānmuhūrtānttu rātrairūrddhvā samāgatā 
sabdhvopavāsināṃ puṇyaṃ svasthā bhava śucismite  NarP 
yamasaṃsthāpanārthāya vaikuṇṭhadhvaṃsanāya ca 
pākhaṇḍānāṃ vivṛddhyarthaṃ pāpasaṃcanāya ca  NarP 
dattaṃ te mohini sthānaṃ pratyūṣasamayāṅkitam  NarP 
viddhaṃ tvayaikādaśikāvrataṃ ye kurvanti kartāra iha prayatnāt 
teṣāṃ bhavedyatsukṛtaṃ śubhe phalaṃ bhuṅkṣva prasannā bhava bhūsure tvam  NarP 
evaṃ pradiṣṭā kamalāsanādyaiḥ sā mohinī hṛṣṭatarā babhūva 
mene kṛtārthaṃ nijajīvitaṃ ca svapāpatīrthābhiniṣevaṇena  NarP 
saṃsādhitaṃ kāryamidaṃ surāṇāṃ bhasmāvaśeṣaṃ hi gate 'pi dehe 
caitanyamātre pavanātmake 'smin saṃmārjito bhūpakṛtastu panthāḥ  NarP 
nītaṃ mayā cātmakṛtaṃ hi vākyaṃ prahṛṣṭayā vai yadudāhṛtaṃ hi 
evaṃ vimṛśya kṣiptipālade vānpraṇamya hṛṣṭā ca purodhasaṃ svam  NarP 
prānte sthitā sūryavihīnasaṃjñe kāle daśamyā janamohanāya 
kṛcchrāntarūpā ca dinaṃ ca bhuṅkte prakṛṣṭarūpā narakāya nṝṇām  NarP 
prāntasthitāṃ tāṃ ravijo nirīkṣya prahṛṣṭavaktro vacanaṃ jagāda

vibhodito rukmavibhūṣaṇasya mattebhasaṃsthaḥ paṭahaḥ sughaiṣaḥ  NarP 
dṛṣṭe kārye janaḥ sarvaḥ pratyayaṃ kurute tviti  NarP 
sūryodaya spṛṣā hyeṣā daśamī garhitā sadā 
aspṛṣṭamudayaṃ nṝṇāṃ mohanāya bhaviṣyati  NarP 
vihāya tāṃ yatpriyayogabhuktiṃ pādasthitā sāpi hyadṛṣyarūpā 
satyaṃ hi te nāma viśālanetre yanmohinītyeva jano bravīti  NarP 
vimohayitvā hi janaṃ samastaṃ paṭe madīye likhitaṃ karoṣi 
ityeva muktvā tanayo vivasvataḥ praṇamya tāṃ brahmasutāṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ  NarP 
jagāma devaiḥ saha nākalokaṃ kare gṛhītvā lipilekhitāram 
gateṣu deveṣu vimohinī sā brahmāṇamāsādya surāsureśam  NarP 
vijñāpayāmāsa pitaḥ purodhā mamāyamatyugrataraśca kopāt 
dagdhaṃ śarīraṃ mama lokanātha punaḥ prapatsye 'tha tathā kuruṣva  NarP 
vimohitaṃ caiva jaganmayedaṃ prānte samāsthāya yamasya tithyāḥ 
jito hi rājñā śamanaḥ purādya kṛto jayī tāta tava prabhāvāt  NarP 
tava kṛtyamidaṃ tāta yatpunardehadhāriṇī 
bhūyāmahaṃ jagannātha brahmaṇaṃ sāṃtyayasva bhoḥ  NarP 
tacchrutvā mohinīvākyaṃ brahmā lokavidhānakṛt 
brāhmaṇaṃ sāṃtvayāmāsa punareva sutākṛte  NarP 
vaso tāta nibodhedaṃ yadbravīmi hitāvaham 
tava cāsyā mahābhāga sarvalokahitāya ca  NarP 
tvayeyaṃ mohinī kopātkṛtā bhasmāvaśeṣitā 
punaḥ śarīraṃ yāceta tadājñāṃ dehi mānada  NarP 
matputrī tava yājyeyaṃ durgatiṃ tāta gacchati 
tvayā mayā ca sapālyā kṛtakāryā tapasvinī  NarP 
yadi tvaṃ śuddhabhāvena māṃ jñāpayasi mānada 
tāto 'hamasyā bhūyo 'pi dehamutpādayāmyaham  NarP 
kintu viṣṇudinasyaiṣā vairiṇī pāpakāriṇī 
yathā śuddhyeti viprendra tathaivāśu vidhīyatām  NarP 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya brahmaṇaḥ sa purohitaḥ 
yājyāyā dehayogārthamādideśa mudānvitaḥ  NarP 
vipravākyaṃ samākarṇya brahmā lokapitamahaḥ 
kamaṇḍalujalenaukṣanmohinyā dehabhasma tat  NarP 
samukṣite brahmaṇā lokakartrā sā mohinī dehayutā babhūva 
praṇamya tātaṃ ca vasoḥ purodhaso jagrāha pādau vinayena natvā  NarP 
tato vasuryājaka eva rājño mudānvito yājyanitaṃbinīṃ tām 
vimohinīṃ svāmisutoñjjhitāṃ ca jagāda vākyaṃ vidutāmavīrām  NarP 
vasuruvāca
krodhastyakto mayā devi brahmaṇo vacanādatha 
gatiṃ te kārayiṣyāmi tīrthasnānādikarmaṇā  NarP 
ityuktvā mohinīṃ vipro brahmāṇāṃ jagatāṃ patim

mohinīṃ samanugrāhyāṃ matvā hṛdi vicārayan  NarP

vasiṣṭaṃ uvāca

uvāca ślakṣṇayā vācā sarvalokahite rataḥ  NarP 
vasuruvāca
śṛṇu mohinī vakṣyāmi tīrthānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthak 
yena vijñātamātreṇa pāpināṃ gatiruttamā  NarP

praṇatā mohinī prāha gaṅgāsnānakṛtādarā  NarP 
mohinyuvāca
bhagavanvāḍavaśreṣṭha gaṅgāmāhātmyamuttamam

śrutvā māhātmyamatulaṃ gaṅgāyāḥ pāpanāśanam

tacchrutvā mohinīvākyaṃ vasuḥ sarvapurāṇavit 
māhātmyaṃ kathayāmāsa gaṅgāyāḥ pāpanāśanam  NarP 
vasuruvāca
te deśāste janapadāste śailā ste 'pi cāśramāḥ 
yeṣāṃ bhāgīrathī puṇyā samīpe vartate sadā  NarP 
tapasā brahmacaryeṇa yajñaistyāgena vā punaḥ 
tāṃ gatiṃ na labhejjanturgaṅgāṃ saṃsevya yāṃ labhet  NarP 
pūrve vayasi pāpāni kṛtvā karmāṇi ye narāḥ 
śeṣe gaṅgāṃ niṣevante te 'pi yānti parāṃ gatim  NarP 
tiṣṭhedyugasahasraṃ tu pādenaikena yaḥ pumān 
māsamekaṃ tu gaṅgāyāṃ snātastulyaphalāvubhau  NarP 
tiṣṭhetārvākchirā yastu yugānāmayutaṃ pumān

bhūtānāmiha sarveṣāṃ duḥkhopahatacetasām

prakṛṣṭaiḥ pātakair ghoraiḥ pāpinaḥ puruṣādhamān 
prasahya tārayedguṅgā gacchato niraye 'śucau  NarP 
te samānāstu munibhirnūnaṃ devaiḥ savāsavaiḥ 
ye 'bhigacchanti satataṃ gaṅgāmabhimatāṃ suraiḥ  NarP 
andhāñjaḍāndravyahīnāṃśca gaṅgā saṃpāvayedbṛhatī viśvarūpā

pakṣādau kṛṣṇapakṣe tu bhūmau saṃnihitā bhavet 
yāvatpuṇyā hyamāvāsyā dināni daśa mohini  NarP 
śuklapratipadādeśca dināni daśa saṃkhyayā 
pātāle sannidhānaṃ tu kurute svayameva hi  NarP

kalau tu sarvatīrthāni svaṃ svaṃ vīryaṃ svabhāvataḥ 
gaṅgāyāṃ pratimuñcanti sā tu devī na kutracit  NarP 
gaṅgāṃbhaḥ kaṇadigdhasya vāyoḥ saṃsparśanādapi

yo 'sau sarvagato viṣṇuścitsvarūpī janārdanaḥ 
sa eva dravarūpeṇa gaṅgāṃbho nātra saṃśayaḥ  NarP 
brahmahā guruḍā goghnaḥ steyī ca gurutalpagaḥ 
gaṅgāṃbhasā ca pūyante nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  NarP 
kṣetrasthamṛddhṛtaṃ vāpi śītamuṣṇamathāpi vā 
gāṅgeyaṃ tu harettoyaṃ pāpamāmaraṇāntikam  NarP 
varjyaṃ paryuṣitaṃ toyaṃ varjyaṃ puryuṣitaṃ dalam 
na varjyaṃ jāhnavītoyaṃ na varjyaṃ tulasīdalam  NarP 
meroḥ suvarṇasya ca sarvaratnaiḥ saṃkhyopalānāmudakasya vāpi

cintāmaṇiguṇāccāpi gaṅgāyāstoyabindavaḥ 
viśiṣṭā yatprayacchanti bhaktebhyo vāñchitaṃ phalam  NarP 
gaṇḍūṣamātrato bhaktyā sakūdgaṅgāṃbhasā naraḥ 
kāmadhenu stanodbhūtānbhuṅkte divyarasāndivi  NarP 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ yastu gaṅgājalaṃ kṣipet

manovākkāyajairgrastaḥ pāpairbahuvidhairapi 
vīkṣya gaṅgāṃ bhavetpūtaḥ puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ  NarP 
gaṅgātoyābhiṣiktāṃ tu bhikṣāmaśnāti yaḥ sadā 
sarpavatkañcukaṃ muktvā pāpahīno bhavetsa vai  NarP 
himavadvindhyasadṛśā rāśayaḥ pāpakarmaṇām

praveśamātre gaṅgāyāṃ snānārthaṃ bhaktito nṛṇām 
brahmahatyādipāpāni hāhetyuktvā prayāntyalam  NarP 
gaṅgātīre vasennityaṃ gaṅgātoyaṃ pibetsadā 
yaḥ pumānsa vimucyeta pātakaiḥ pūrvasaṃcitaiḥ  NarP 
yo vai gaṅgāṃ samāśritya nityaṃ tiṣṭhati nirbhayaḥ 
sa eva devairmartyaiśca pūjanīyo maharṣibhiḥ  NarP 
kimaṣṭāṅgena yogena kiṃ tapobhiḥ kimadhvaraiḥ 
vāsa eva hi gaṅgāyāṃ sarvato 'pi viśiṣyate  NarP 
kiṃ yajñairbahubhirjāpyaiḥ kiṃ tapobhirdhanārpaṇaiḥ 
svargamokṣapradā gaṅgā sukhasevyā yataḥ sthitā  NarP 
yajñairyamaiśca niyamairdānaiḥ saṃnyāsato 'pi vā 
na tatphalamavāproti gaṅgāṃ sevya yadāpnuyāt  NarP 
prabhāse gosahastreṇa rāhugraste divākare 
yatphalaṃ labhate martyo gaṅgāyāṃ taddinena vai  NarP 
anyopāyāṃśca yastyaktvā mīkṣakāmaḥ suniścitaḥ 
gaṅgātīre sukhaṃ tiṣṭhetsa vai mokṣasya bhājanam  NarP 
vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣaṇa gaṅgā sadyastu mokṣadā 
pratimāsaṃ caturdaśyāmaṣṭamyāṃ caiva sarvadā  NarP 
gaṅgātīre nivāsaśca yāvajjīvaṃ ca siddhidaḥ 
kṛcchrāṇi sarvadā kṛtvā yatphalaṃ sukhamaśnute  NarP 
sadā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caiva tallabhejjāhnavītaṭe

na tacchakyaṃ brahmasute prāptuṃ kratuśatairapi 
sarvayajñatapodānayogasvādhyāyakarmabhiḥ  NarP 
yatphalaṃ tallabhedbhaktyā gaṅgātīranivāsataḥ 
yatpuṇyaṃ satyavacanairnaiṣṭhikabrahmacāriṇām  NarP 
yadagnihotriṇāṃ puṇyaṃ tattu gaṅgānivāsataḥ 
samātṛpitṛdārāṇāṃ kulakoṭimanantakam  NarP 
gaṅgābhaktistārayate saṃsārārṇavato dhruvam

tadbhaktastatparaśca syānmṛto vāpi na saṃśayaḥ 
bhaktyā tajjalasaṃsparśī tajjalaṃ pibate ca yaḥ  NarP 
anāyāsena hi naro mokṣo pāyaṃ sa vindati 
dīkṣitaḥ sarvayajñeṣu somapānaṃ dine dine  NarP 
sarvāṇi yaṃṣāṃ gaṅgāyāstoyaiḥ kṛtyāni sarvadā

devāḥ somārkasaṃsthāni yathā śakrādayo mukhaiḥ 
amṛtānyupabhuñjanti tathā gaṅgājalaṃ narāḥ  NarP 
kanyādānaiśca vidhivadbhūmidānaiśca bhaktitaḥ 
annadānaiśca godānaiḥ svarṇadānādibhistathā  NarP 
rathāśvagajadānaiśca yatpuṇyaṃ parikīrtitam

tribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ saptabhistvatha yāmunam

śāstreṇākṛtatoyānāṃ mṛtānāṃ kvāpi dehanām

vasuruvāca
śṛṇu mohini vakṣyāmi gaṅgāyā darśane phalam 
yaduktaṃ hi purāṇeṣu munibhistattvadarśibhiḥ  NarP 
bhavanti nirviṣāḥ sarpā yathā tārkṣyasya daśa nāt 
gaṅgāsaṃdarśanāttadvatsarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  NarP 
saptāvarān saptaparān pitṛṃstebhyaśca ye pare

darśanātsparśanātpānāttathā gaṅgeti kīrtanāt 
pumānpunāti puruṣāñchataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ  NarP 
jñānamaiśvaryamatulaṃ pratiṣṭhāyuryaśastathā 
śubhānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca gaṅgādarśanajaṃ phalam  NarP 
sarvendriyāṇāṃ cāñcalyaṃ vyasanāni ca pātakam 
nirghṛṇatvaṃ ca naśyanti gaṅgādarśana mātrataḥ  NarP 
parahiṃsā ca kauṭilyaṃ paradoṣādyavekṣaṇam 
dāṃbhikatvaṃ nṛṇāṃ gaṅgādarśanādeva naśyati  NarP 
muhurmuhustathā paśyetspṛśedvāpi muhurmuhuḥ 
bhaktyā yadicchati naraḥ śāśvataṃ padamavyayam  NarP 
vāpīkūpataḍāgādiprapāsatrādibhistathā 
anyatra yadbhavetpuṇyaṃ tadgaṅgādarśanādbhavet  NarP 
yatphalaṃ jāyate puṃsāṃ darśane paramātmanaḥ 
tadbhavedeva gaṅgāyā darśanādbhaktibhāvataḥ  NarP 
naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre narmadāyāṃ ca puṣkare 
snānātsaṃsparśanā sevya yatphalaṃ labhate naraḥ  NarP 
tadgaṅgādarśanādeva kalau prāhurmaharṣayaḥ 
atha te smaraṇasyāpi gaṅgāyā bhūpabhāmini  NarP 
pravakṣyāmi phalaṃ yattu purāṇeṣu prakīrtitam 
aśubhaiḥ karmabhiryuktānmajjamānānbhavārṇave  NarP 
patato narake gaṅgā smṛtā dūrātsamuddharet 
yojanānāṃ sahasreṣu gaṅgāṃ smarati yo naraḥ  NarP 
api duṣkṛtakarmā hi labhate paramāṃ gatim 
smaraṇādeva gaṅgāyāḥ pāpasaṃghātapañjaram  NarP 
bhedaṃ sahasradhā yāti girirvajrahato yathā 
gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapandhyāyañjāgradbhuñjan hasan rudan  NarP 
yaḥ smaretsatataṃ gaṅgāṃ sa ca mucyeta bandhanāt 
sahasrayojanasthāśca gaṅgāṃ bhaktyā smaranti ye  NarP 
gaṅgāgaṅgeti cākruśya mucyante te 'pi pātakāt 
ye ca smaranti vai gaṅgāṃ gaṅgābhaktiparāśca ye  NarP 
te 'pyaśeṣairmahāpāpairmucyante nātra saṃśayaḥ 
bhavanāni vicitrāṇi vicitrābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ  NarP 
ārogyaṃ vittrasaṃpattirgaṅgāsmaraṇañja phalam 
manasā saṃsmaredyastu gaṅgāṃ dūrasthito naraḥ  NarP 
cāndrāyaṇasahasrasya sa phalaṃ labhate dhruvam 
gaṅgā gaṅgā japannāma yojanānāṃ śate sthitaḥ  NarP 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati 
kīrtanānmucyate pāpāddarśanānmaṅgalaṃ labhet  NarP 
avagāhya tathā pītvā punātyāsaptamaṃ kulam 
saptāvaparānparānsapta saptātha parataḥ parān  NarP 
gaṅgā tārayate puṃsāṃ prasaṃgenāpi kīrtitā 
aśraddhayāpi gaṅgāyā yattu nāmānukīrtanam  NarP 
karoti puṇyavāhinyāḥ so 'pi svargasya bhājanam 
sarvāvasthāṃ gato vāpi sarvadharmavivarjitaḥ  NarP 
gaṅgāyāḥ kīrtanenaiva śubhāṃ gatimavāpnuyāt 
brahmahā guruhāgoghnaḥ spṛṣṭo vā sarvapātakaiḥ  NarP 
gaṅgātoyaṃ naraḥ spṛṣṭvā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ 
kadā drakṣyāmi tāṃ gaṅgāṃ kadā snānaṃ labhe hyaham  NarP 
iti puṃsābhilaṣitā kulānāṃ tārayecchatam 
atha snānaphalaṃ devi gaṅgāyāḥ pravadāmi te  NarP 
yacchrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
snātasya gaṅgāsalile sadyaḥ pāpaṃ praṇaśyati  NarP 
apūrvapuṇyaprāptiśca sadyo mohini jāyate 
snātānāṃ śucibhistoyairgāṅgeyaiḥ prayatātmanām  NarP 
vyuṣṭirbhavati yā puṃsāṃ na sā kratuśatairapi 
apahatya tamastīvraṃ yathā bhātyudaye raviḥ  NarP 
tathāpahatya pāpmānaṃ bhāti gaṅgājalokṣitaḥ 
ekenaivāpi vidhinā snānena nṛpasundari  NarP 
aśvamedhaphalaṃ martyo gaṅgāyāṃ labhate dhruvam 
anekajanmasaṃbhūtaṃ puṃsaḥ pāpaṃ praṇaśyati  NarP 
snānamātreṇa gaṅgāyāḥ sadyaḥ syātpuṇyabhājanam 
anyasthānakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ gaṅgātīre vinaśyati  NarP 
gaṅgātīre kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ gaṅgāsnānena naśyati 
rātrau divā ca saṃdhyāyāṃ gaṅgāyāṃ tu prayatnataḥ  NarP 
snātvāśvamedhajaṃ puṇyaṃ gṛhe 'pyuddhṛtatatajjalaiḥ 
sarvatīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ sarveṣṭāyataneṣu ca  NarP 
tatphalaṃ labhate martyo gaṅgāsnānānna saṃśayaḥ 
mahāpātakasaṃyukto yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ  NarP 
gaṅgāsnānena vidhivanmucyate sarvapātakaiḥ 
gaṅgā snānātparaṃ snānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati  NarP 
viśeṣataḥ kaliyuge pāpaṃ harati jāhnavī 
nihatya kāmajāndoṣānkāyavākcittasaṃbhavān  NarP 
gaṅgāsnānena bhaktyā tu modate divi devavat 
varṣaṃ snāti ca gaṅgāyāṃ yo naro bhaktisaṃyutaḥ  NarP 
tasya syādvaiṣṇave loke sthitiḥ kalpaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
āmṛtyuṃ snāti gaṅgāyāṃ yo naro nityameva ca  NarP 
samastapāpanimuktaḥ samastakulasaṃyutaḥ 
samastabhogasaṃyukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate  NarP 
parārddhadvitayaṃ yāvannātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
gaṅgāyāṃ snāti yo martyo nairantaryeṇa nityadā  NarP 
jīvanmuktaḥ sa cātraiva mṛto viṣṇupadaṃ vrajet 
prātaḥsnānāddaśaguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ madhyandine smṛtam  NarP 
sāyaṅkāle śataguṇamanantaṃ śivasannidhau 
kapilākoṭidānāddhi gaṅgāsnānaṃ viśiṣyate  NarP 
kurukṣetrasamā gaṅgā yatra tatrāvagāhitā 
haridvāre prayāge ca siṃdhusaṃge phalādhikā  NarP 
ye madīyāṃśusaṃtapte jale te snānti jāhnavi 
te bhitvā maṇḍalaṃ yānti mokṣaṃ ceti ravervacaḥ  NarP 
yo gṛhe sve sthito 'pi tvāṃ snāne saṃkīrtayiṣyati 
so 'pi yāsyati nākaṃ vai ityāha varuṇaśca tām  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite gaṅgāsnānamāhātmyaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
vasuruvāca
atha kālaviśeṣe tu gaṅgāsnānasya te phalam 
kīrtayiṣyāmi vāmoru sāvadhānā niśāmaya  NarP 
nairantaryeṇa gaṅgāyā māghe snāti ca yo naraḥ 
saśakraloke suciraṃ kālaṃ tiṣṭhetsagotrajaḥ  NarP 
tato brahmapuraṃ yāti kalpakoṭiśatāyutaiḥ 
nairantaryeṇa vidhivadgaṅgāyāṃ snāti yo naraḥ  NarP 
ṣaṇmāsa mekakālāśī sakṛdevottarāyaṇe 
so 'pi viṣṇupadaṃ yāti kulānāṃ śatamuddharan  NarP 
saṃkrāntiṣu tu sarvāsu snātvā gaṅgājale naraḥ 
vimānenārkavarṇena sa vrajedviṣṇumandiram  NarP 
viṣuve 'yanasaṃkrāntau viśeṣātphalamīritam 
tapaḥsamaṃ kārtike 'pi gaṅgāsnāne phalaṃ viduḥ  NarP 
meṣapraveśārkakāle kārtikyāṃ vāpi mohini 
māghasnānādhikaṃ prāhuḥ kamalāsanapūrvakāḥ  NarP 
saṃvatsarasnānajanyaṃ phalamakṣayake tithau 
kārtike vāpi vaiśākhe iti prāha pitā tava  NarP 
manvādau ca yugādau yatproktaṃ gaṅgājale phalam 
snānaina yājyavanite trimāsyāpi ca tatphalam  NarP 
dvādaśyāṃ śravaṇarkṣe ca aṣṭabhyāṃ puṣyayogataḥ 
ārdrāyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ gaṅgāsnānaṃ sudurlabham  NarP 
pūrṇimā mādhave puṇyā tathā kārtikamāghayoḥ 
amāvasyāstathaiteṣāṃ gaṅgāsnāne sudurlabhāḥ  NarP 
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ sahasraṃ tu śataṃ syātsarvaparvasu 
amāyāṃ ca tathāṣṭamyāṃ māghāsitadale sati  NarP 
ardhodayaṃ tadā parvakiñcinnyūnaṃ mahodayaḥ 
mahodaye śataguṇaṃ lakṣamarddhodaye smṛtam  NarP 
snānaṃ gaṅgājale devi grahaṇāccandrasūryayoḥ 
māsatrayasnānaphalaṃ phālgunāṣāḍha māsayoḥ  NarP 
janmarkṣe tu kṛte snāne gaṅgāyāṃ bhaktibhāvataḥ 
janmaprabhṛti pāpaṃ vai saṃcitaṃ hi vinaśyati  NarP 
caturdaśyāṃ māghakṛṣṇe vyatīpātaśca durlabhaḥ 
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ viśeṣeṇa vaidhṛtirjāhnavījale  NarP 
māghaṃ sakalamevāpi naro yo vidhipūrvakam 
aruṇodayake snāyī sa tu jātismaro bhavet  NarP 
sarvaśāstrārthavijjñānī nīrogaśca bhavedbhruvam 
saṃkrāntyāṃ pakṣayorante grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ  NarP 
gaṅgāsnāto naraḥ kāmādbrahmaṇaḥ sadanaṃ labhet 
indorlakṣaguṇaṃ proktaṃ raverdaśaguṇaṃ tataḥ  NarP 
gaṅgātīre tu saṃprāptā indoḥ koṭī raverdaśa 
vāruṇena samāyuktā madhau kṛṣṇā trayodaśī 
gaṅgāyāṃ yadi labhyeta sūryagrahaśataiḥ samā  NarP 
jyeṣṭhe māsi kṣitisutadine śuklapakṣe daśamyāṃ haste śailādavataradasau jāhnavī martyalokam 
pāpānyasyāṃ harati hi tithau sā daśaiṣādyagaṅgā puṇyaṃ dadyādapi śataguṇaṃ vājimedhakratośca  NarP 
mahāpātakasaṃghāni yāni pāpāni saṃti me 
govindadvādaśīṃ prāpya tāni me hana jāhnavi  NarP 
maghāsaṃjñena ṛkṣeṇa candraḥ saṃpūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ 
guruṇā yāti saṃyogaṃ tanmahatvaṃ titheḥ smṛtam  NarP 
gaṅgāyāṃ yadi labhyeta sūryagrahaśataiḥ samā 
atha deśaviśeṣeṇa snānasya phalamucyate  NarP 
kurukṣetrāddaśaguṇā yatra tatrāvagāhitā 
kurukṣetrācchataguṇā yatra vindhyena saṃyutā  NarP 
vindhyācchataguṇā proktā kāśīpuryāṃ tu jāhnavī 
sarvatra durlabhā gaṅgā triṣu sthāneṣu cādhikā  NarP 
gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṃgame 
eṣu snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste 'punarbhavāḥ  NarP 
gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte snāne puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu 
saptānāṃ rājasūyānāṃ phalaṃ syādaśvamedhayoḥ  NarP 
uṣitvā tatra māsārddhaṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ viśvajitāṃ phalam 
daśāyutānāṃ tu gavāṃ dānapuṇyaṃ vidurbudhāḥ  NarP 
sarottame 'tha govindaṃ rudraṃ kanakhale sthitam 
snātvā vāpyeṣu gaṅgāyāṃ puṇyamakṣayamāpnuyāt  NarP 
tīrthaṃ ca saukaraṃ nāma mahāpuṇyaṃ śubhe śṛṇu 
yasminnāvirabhūtpūrvaṃ vārāhākṛtiracyutaḥ  NarP 
śatasyāgnicitāṃ puṇyaṃ jyotiṣṭomadvayasya ca 
agniṣṭomasahasrasya phalamāpnoti mānavaḥ  NarP 
tatraiva brahmaṇastīrthe jyotiṣṭomāyutasya ca 
aśvamedhatrayasyāpi snātaḥ puṇyaṃ labhennaraḥ  NarP 
kubjākhyaṃ tīrthamanaghaṃ yatra ca vyādhayo 'khilāḥ 
naśyanti sarvajanmotthaṃ pātakaṃ cāpi mohini  NarP 
atrānyatkāpilaṃ tīrthaṃ yatra snāto naraḥ śubhe 
kapilāṣṭāyutasyāpi dānatulyaphalaṃ labhet  NarP 
gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte bilvake nīlaparvate 
tīrthe kanakhale snātvā dhūtapāpo vrajeddivam  NarP 
pavitrārthaṃ tatastīrthaṃ sarvatīrthottamottamam 
dvayorviśvajitostatra snānātpuṇyaṃ labhennaraḥ  NarP 
veṇīrājyaṃ tatastīrthaṃ sarayūryatra gaṅgayā 
supuṇyayā mahāpuṇyā svasā svasreva saṃgatā  NarP 
harerdakṣiṇapādābjakṣālanādamarāpagā 
vāmapādodbhavā vāpi sarayūrmānasaprasūḥ  NarP 
tīrthe tatrārcayan rudraṃ viṣṇuṃ viṣṇutvamāpnuyāt 
pañcāśvamedhaphaladaṃ snānaṃ tatra prakīrtitam  NarP 
tatastu gāṇḍavaṃ tīrthaṃ gaṇḍakī yatra saṃgatā 
gosahasrasya dānaṃ ca tatra snānaṃ samaṃ dvayam  NarP 
rāmatīrthaṃ tataḥ puṇyaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ yatra sannidhau 
somatīrthaṃ tataḥ puṇyaṃ yatrāsau nakulo muniḥ  NarP 
samabhyarcya śivaṃ dhyāyangaṇatāṃ tu samāyayau 
caṃpakākhyaṃ puṇyatīrthaṃ yadgaṅgottaravāhinī  NarP 
maṇikarṇikayā tulyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam 
kalaśākhyaṃ tatastīrthaṃ kalaśādutthito muniḥ  NarP 
agastyaḥ pūjayanyatra rudraṃ munivaro 'bhavat 
somadvīpaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ tīrthaṃ vārāṇasīsamam  NarP 
somo yatrārcayannīśaṃ rudreṇa śirasā dhṛtaḥ 
viśvāmitrasya bhaginī gaṅgayā yatra saṃgatā  NarP 
tatrāpluto naro bhūyādvāsavasya priyo 'tithiḥ 
jahnuhrade mahātīrthe snāto martyo hi mohini  NarP 
ekaviṃśatikulyānāṃ tārako bhavati dhruvam 
tasmādadititīrthaṃ ca yatrāvāpāditirharim  NarP 
kaśyapāttatra subhage snānamāhurmahodayam 
śiloccayaṃ mahātīrthaṃ yatra taptvā tapaḥ prajāḥ  NarP 
tṛṇādibhiḥ saha svargaṃ yānti tīrthagaṇāśrayāt 
indrāṇīnāmatīrthaṃ syādyatrendrāṇī tu vāsavam  NarP 
tapastaptvā patiṃ lebhe sevyametatprayāgavat 
puṇyadaṃ snātakaṃ tīrthaṃ viśvāmitrastapaścaran  NarP 
yatra brahmarṣitāṃ lebhe kṣattriyastīrthā sevayā 
pradyumnatīrthaṃ tapasā khyātaṃ yatra smaro hareḥ  NarP 
pradyumnanāmā putro 'bhūtparaṃ tatra mahodayam 
tato dakṣaprayāgaṃ tu gaṅgāto yamunāgata  NarP 
snātvā tatrākṣayaṃ puṇyaṃ prayāga iva labhyate  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīvasusaṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye sthalaviśeṣasnānaphalakathanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
vasuruvāca
athāvagāhanādīnāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalamucyate 
sāvadhānā śṛṇuṣva tvaṃ brahmaputri nṛpapriye  NarP 
yaiḥ puṇyavāhinī gaṅgā sakṛdbhaktyāvagāhitā 
teṣāṃ kulānāṃ lakṣaṃ tu bhavāttārayate śivā  NarP 
sāmānyasthānato devi tatra saṃdhyā hyupāsitā 
puṇyaṃ lakṣaguṇaṃ kartuṃ samarthā dvijapāvanī  NarP 
dattāḥ pitṛbhyo yatrāpastanayaiḥ śraddhayānvitaiḥ 
akṣayāṃ tu prakurvanti tṛptiṃ mohini durlabhām  NarP 
yāvantaśca tilā martyārgṛhītāḥ pitṛkarmaṇi 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi pitaraḥ svargavāsinaḥ  NarP 
pitṛlokeṣu ye kecitsarveṣāṃ pitaraḥ sthitāḥ 
tarpyamāṇāḥ parāṃ tṛptiṃ yānti gaṅgājalaiḥ śubhaiḥ  NarP 
ya icchetsaphalaṃ janma saṃtatiṃ vā śubhānane 
sa pitṝṃstarpayedgaṅgāmabhigamya surāṃstathā  NarP 
ye matā durgatā martyāstarpitāstatkulodbhavaiḥ 
kuśaistilairgāṅgajalaiste prayānti hareḥ padam  NarP 
svargasasthāśca ye kecitpitaraḥ puṇyaśīlinaḥ 
te tarpitā gāṅgajalairmokṣe yānti vidhervacaḥ  NarP 
māsaṃ tarpaṇamātreṇa piṇḍasaṃpātanena ca 
gaṅgāyāṃ pitaraḥ sarve suprītāḥ sūryavarcasaḥ  NarP 
apsaro gaṇaṇasaṃyuktānhemaratnavibhūṣitān 
muktājālaparicchannānveṇuvīṇānināditān  NarP 
bherīśaṅkhamṛdaṅgādinirghoṣānsragvibhūṣitān 
gandharvadeharucirāndivyabhogasamanvitān  NarP  
āruhya tu vimānāgryānbrahyalokaṃ prayānti hi 
gaṅgāyāṃ tu naraḥ snātvā yo nityaṃ liṅgamarcayet  NarP 
ekena janmanā mokṣaṃ paramānpoti sa dhruvam 
agnihotrāṇi vedāśca yajñāśca bahudakṣiṇāḥ  NarP 
gaṅgāyāṃ liṅgapūjāyāḥ koṭyaṃśenāpi no samāḥ 
pitṝnudiśya vā devāngaṅgāṃbhibhiḥ prasiṃcayet  NarP 
tṛptāḥ syustasya pitaro narakasthāśca tatkṣaṇāt 
mṛtkuṃbhāttāmrakuṃbhaistu snānaṃ daśaguṇaṃ smṛtam  NarP 
raupyaiḥ śataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ hemaiḥ koṭiguṇaṃ smṛtam 
evamarghe ca naivedye balipūjādiṣu kramāt  NarP 
pātrāṃ taraviśeṣeṇa phalaṃ caivottarottaram 
vibhave sati yo mohānna kuryādvidhivistaram  NarP 
na sa tatkarmaphalabhāgdevadrohī prakīrtyate 
devānāṃ darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ darśanātsparśanaṃ varam  NarP 
sparśanādarcanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ ghṛtasnānamataḥ param 
prāhurgaṅgājalaiḥ snānaṃ ghṛtasnānasamaṃ budhāḥ  NarP 
arghyaṃ dravyaviśeṣeṇa gaṅgātoyena yaḥ sakṛt 
māgadhaprasthamātreṇa tāmrapātrasthitena ca  NarP 
devatābhyaḥ pradadyāttu svakīyapitṛbhiḥ saha 
putrapautraiśca saṃyuktaḥ sa ca vai svargamāpnuyāt 
āpaḥ kṣīraṃ kuśāgrāṇi ghṛtaṃ dadhi tathā madhu  NarP 
raktāni karavīrāṇi tathā vai raktacandanam 
aṣṭāṅgaireṣa yuktor'gho bhānave parikīrtitaḥ  NarP 
viṣṇoḥ śivasya sūryyasya durgāyā brahmaṇastathā 
gaṅgātīre pratiṣṭhāṃ tu yaḥ karoti narottamaḥ  NarP 
tathaivāyatanānyeṣāṃ kārayatyapi śaktitaḥ 
anyatīrtheṣu karaṇātkoṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  NarP 
gaṅgātīrasamudbhūtamṛdā ligāni śaktitaḥ 
salakṣaṇāni kṛtvā tu pratiṣṭhāpya dine dine  NarP 
mantreśca patrapuṣpādyaiḥ pūjayitvā ca śaktitaḥ 
gaṅgāyāṃ nikṣipennityaṃ tasya pupayamanantakam  NarP 
sarvānandapradāyinyāṃ gaṅgāyāṃ yo narottamaḥ 
aṣṭākṣaraṃ japedbhaktya muktistasya kare sthitā  NarP 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti praṇavādyaṃ niyamya ca 
ṣaṇmāsaṃ japataḥ sarvā hyupatiṣṭhanti siddhayaḥ  NarP 
namaḥ śivāyeti mantraṃ satāraṃ vidhinā tu yaḥ 
caturviśatilakṣaṃ vai japetsākṣātsaśaṅkaraḥ  NarP 
pañcākṣarī siddhavidyā śiva eva na saṃśayaḥ 
apavitraḥ pavitro vā japanniṣpātako bhavet  NarP 
pūjitāyāṃ tu gaṅgāyāṃ pūjitāḥ sarva devatāḥ 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena pūjayedamarāpagām  NarP 
caturbhujāṃ trinetrāṃ ca sarvāvayavaśobhitām 
ratnakuṃbhasitāṃbhojavarābhayakaraṃ śubhām  NarP 
śvetavastraparīdhānāṃ muktāmaṇivibhūṣitām 
suprasannāṃ suvadanāṃ karuṇārdrahṛdaṃbujām  NarP 
sudhāplāvitabhūpṛṣṭhāṃ trailokyanamitāṃ sadā 
dhyātvā jalamayīṃ gaṅgāṃ pūjayanpuṇyabhāgbhavet  NarP 
māsārddhamapi yastvevaṃ nairantaryeṇa pūjayet 
sa eva devasadṛśo bahukāle phalādhikaḥ  NarP 
vaiśākhaśuklasaptamyāṃ jahnunā jāhnavī purā 
krodhātpītā punastyaktā karṇaraṅghrāttu dakṣiṇāt  NarP 
tāṃ tatra pūjayeddevīṃ gaṅgāṃ gaganamekhalām

caturbhujāṃ sunetrāṃ ca candrāyutasamaprabhām  NarP 
cāmarairvījyamānāṃ ca śvetacchatropaśibhitām 
suprasannāṃ ca varadāṃ karuṇārdranijāntarām  NarP 
sudhāplāvitabhūpṛṣṭhāṃ devādibhirabhiṣṭutām 
divyaratnaparītāṃ ca diṃvyamālyānulepanām  NarP 
dhyātvā jale yathāproktāṃ tatrārcāyāṃ tu pūjayet 
vakṣyamāṇena mantreṇa kuryātpūjāṃ viśeṣataḥ  NarP 
pañcāmṛtena ca snānamarcāyāṃ tu viśiṣyate 
pratimāgre sthaṇḍile tu gomayenopalepayet  NarP 
nārāyaṇaṃ maheśaṃ ca brahmāṇaṃ bhāskaraṃ tathā 
bhagīrathaṃ ca nṛpatiṃ himavantaṃ nageśvaram  NarP 
gandhapuṣpādibhiścaiva yathāśakti prapūjayet 
daśaprasthāṃ stilāndadyāddaśa viprebhya eva ca  NarP 
daśaprasthānyavāndadyāddaśa gavyairyathāhitān 
matsyakacchapamaṇḍūkamarādijalecarān  NarP 
kāritānvai yathāśakti svarṇena rajatena vā 
tadalābhe piṣṭamayānabhyarcya kusumādibhiḥ 
gaṅgāyāṃ prakṣipetpūrvvaṃ mantreṇaiva tu mantravit  NarP 
rathayātrādine tasminvibhave sati kārayet 
rathārūḍhapratikṛtiṃ gaṅgāyāstūttarāmukhām  NarP 
bhramantyā darśanaṃ loke durlabhaṃ pāpakarmaṇām 
durgāyā rathayātrāsti tathaivātrāpi kārayet  NarP 
evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ 
daśapāpairvakṣyamāṇaiḥ sadya eva vimucyate  NarP 
adattānāmupādānaṃ hiṃsā caivāvidhānataḥ 
paradāropasevā ca kāyikaṃ tribidhaṃ smṛtam  NarP 
pāṃruṣyamanṛtaṃ vāpi paiśunyaṃ cāpi sarvaśaḥ 
asaṃbaddhapralāpaśca vācikaṃ syāccaturvidham  NarP 
paradravyeṣvabhidhyānaṃ manasāniṣṭacintanam 
vitathābhiniveśaśca mānasaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam  NarP 
etairdaśavidhaiḥ pāpaiḥ koṭijanmasamudbhavaiḥ 
mucyate nātra saṃdeho brahmaṇo vacanaṃ yathā  NarP 
daśa triṃśacca tānpūrvānpitṝneva tathāparān 
uddharatyeva saṃsārānmantreṇānena pūjitā  NarP 
oṃ namo daśaharāyai nārāyaṇyai gaṅgāyai namaḥ 
iti mantreṇa yo martyo dine tasmindivāniśam  NarP 
japetpacasahasrāṇi daśadharmaphalaṃ labhet 
uddareddaśa pūrvāṇi parāṇi ca bhavārṇavāt  NarP 
vakṣyamāṇamidaṃ stotraṃ vidhinā pratigṛhya ca 
gaṅgāgre taddine japyaṃ viṣṇupūjāṃ pravartayet  NarP 
oṃ namaḥ śivāyai gaṅgāyai śivadāyai namo 'stu te 
namo 'stu viṣṇurūpiṇyai gaṅgāyai te namo namaḥ  NarP 
sarvadevasvarūpiṇyai namo bheṣajamūrtaye 
sarvasya sarvavyādhīnāṃ bhiṣakśreṣṭhe namo 'stu te  NarP 
sthāṇujaṅgamasaṃbhūtaviṣahantri namo 'stu te 
saṃsāraviṣanāśinyai jīvanāyai namonamaḥ  NarP 
tāpatritayahantryai ca prāṇeśvaryai namonamaḥ 
śāntyai saṃtāpahāriṇyai namaste sarvamūrtaye  NarP 
sarvasaṃśuddhikāriṇyai namaḥ pāpavimuktaye 
bhuktimuktipradāyinyai bhogavatyai namonamaḥ  NarP 
mandākinyai namaste 'stu svargadāyai namonamaḥ 
namastrailokyamūrtāyai tridaśāyai namonamaḥ  NarP 
namaste śuklasaṃsthāyai kṣemavatyai namonamaḥ 
tridaśāsanasaṃsthāyai tejovatyai namo 'stu te  NarP 
mandāyai liṅgadhāriṇyai nārāyaṇyai namonamaḥ 
namaste viśvamitrāyai revatyai te namonamaḥ  NarP 
bṛhatyai te namo nityaṃ lokadhātryai namonamaḥ 
namaste viśvamukhyāyai nandinyai te namonamaḥ  NarP 
pṛthvyai śivāmṛtāyai ca virajāyai namonamaḥ 
parāvaragatādyaiyai tārāyai te namonamaḥ  NarP 
namaste svargasaṃsthāyai abhinnāyai namonamaḥ 
śāntāyai te pratiṣṭhāyai varadāyai namonamaḥ  NarP 
ugrāyai nukhajalpāyai saṃjīvinyai namonamaḥ 
brahmagāyai brahmadāyai duritaghnyai namonamaḥ  NarP 
praṇatārtiprabhañjinyai jaganmātre namonamaḥ 
viluṣāyai durgahantryai dakṣāyai te namonamaḥ  NarP 
sarvāpatpratipakṣāyai maṅgalāyai namonamaḥ 
parāpare pare tubhya namo mokṣaprade sadā 
gaṅgā mamāgrato bhūyādgaṅgā me pārśvayostathā  NarP 
gaṅgā me sarvato bhūyāttvayi gaṅge 'stu me sthitiḥ 
ādau tvamante madhye ca sarvā tvaṃ gāṅgate śive  NarP 
tvameva mūlaprakṛtistvaṃ hi nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ 
gaṅge tvaṃ paramātmā ca śivastubhyaṃ namonamaḥ  NarP 
itīdaṃ paṭhati stotraṃ nityaṃ bhaktiparastu yaḥ 
śṛṇoti śraddhayā vāpi kāyavācikasaṃbhavaiḥ  NarP 
daśadhā saṃsthitairdeṣaiḥ sarvaireva pramucyate 
rogī pramucyate rogānmucyetāpanna āpadaḥ  NarP 
dviṣabhdyo bandhanāccāpi bhayebhyaśca vimucyate 
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti pretya brahmaṇi līyate  NarP 
idaṃ stotraṃ gṛhe yasya likhitaṃ paripūjyate 
nāgnicaurabhayaṃ tatra pāpebhyo 'pi bhayaṃ nahi  NarP 
tasyāṃ daśamyāmetacca stotraṃ gaṅgājale sthitaḥ 
japaṃstu daśakṛtvaśca daridro vāpi cākṣamaḥ  NarP 
so 'pi tatphalamāpnoti gaṅgāṃ saṃpūjya bhaktitaḥ 
pūrvoktena vidhānena phalaṃ yatparikīrtitam  NarP 
yathā gaurī tathā gaṅgā tasmādgauryāstu pūjane 
vidhiryo vihitaḥ samyakso 'pi gaṅgāprapūjane  NarP 
yathā śivastathā viṣṇuryathā viṣṇustathā hyumā 
umā yathā tathā gaṅgā cātra bhedo na vidyate  NarP 
viṣṇurudrāntaraṃ yaśca gagāgauryantaraṃ tathā 
lakṣmīgauryataraṃ yaśca prabrūte mūḍhadhīstu saḥ  NarP 
śuklapakṣe divā bhūmau gaṅgāyāmuttarāyaṇe 
dhanyā dehaṃ vimuñcanti hṛdayasthe janārdane  NarP 
ye muñcanti narāprāṇān gaṅgāyāṃ vidhinaṃ dini 
te viṣṇulokaṃ gacchanti stūyamānā divisthitaiḥ  NarP 
arddhodakena jāhnavyāṃ mniyate 'naśanena yaḥ 
sa yāti na punarjanma brahmasāyujyameti ca  NarP 
yā gatiryogayuktasya sātvikasya manīṣiṇaḥ 
sā getistyajataḥ prāṇān gaṅgāyāṃ tu śarīriṇaḥ  NarP 
anaśanaṃ gṛhītvā yo gaṅgātīre mṛto naraḥ 
satyameva paraṃ lokamāpnoti pitṛbhiḥ saha  NarP 
gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇātprāṇānyoḥ prājñastyaktumicchati 
gatāni bahujanmāni yatra yatra mṛtāni ca  NarP 
mahāṃścāpi gataḥ kālo yatra tatrāpi gacchataḥ 
atradūre samīpe ca sadṛśaṃ yojanadvayam  NarP 
gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇeneha nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
jñānato 'jñānato vāpi kāmato 'pi vā  NarP 
gaṅgāyāṃ tu mṛto martyaḥ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ ca vindati 
prāṇeṣūtsṛjyamāneṣu yo gaṅgāṃ saṃsmarennaraḥ  NarP 
spṛśedvā pāpaśīlo 'pi sa vai yāti parāṃ gatim  NarP 
gaṅgāṃ gatvā yaiḥ śarīraṃ visṛṣṭaṃ prāptā dhīrāste tu devaiḥ samatvam 
tasmātsurvānprohya muktipradānvai sevedgaṅgāmā śarīrasya pātam  NarP 
antarikṣe kṣitau toye pāpīyānapi yo mṛtaḥ 
brahmaviṣṇuśivaiḥ pūjyaṃ padamakṣayyamaśnute  NarP 
yo dharmiśṭaśca saprāṇaḥ prayataḥ śiṣṭasaṃmataḥ 
cintayenmanasā gaṅgāṃ sa gatiṃ paramāṃ labhet  NarP 
yatra tatra mṛto vāpi maraṇe samupasthite 
bhaktyā gaṅgāṃ smaranyāti śaivaṃ vā vaiṣṇavaṃ puram  NarP 
śaṃbhorjaṭākalāpāttu viniṣkrāntātikarkaśāt 
plāvayitvā divaṃ ninye yā pāpānyagarātmajān  NarP 
yāvantyasthīni gaṅgāyāṃ tiṣṭhanti puruṣasya vai 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate  NarP 
gagātoye tu yasyāsthi nītvā prakṣipyate naraiḥ 
tatkālamāditaḥ kṛtvā svargaloke bhavetsthitiḥ  NarP 
gaṅgātoye tu yasyāsthi prāpyate śubhakarmaṇaḥ 
na tasya punarāvṛttirbrahmalokātkathañcana  NarP 
daśāhābhyantare yasya gaṅgātoye 'sthi saṃgatam 
gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇe yādṛktādṛkphalamavāpnuyāt  NarP 
snātvā tataḥ pañcagavyena siktvā hiraṇyamadhvājyatilairniyojya 
tadasthipiṇḍaṃ puṭake nidhāya paśyan diśaṃ pretagaṇopagūḍhām  NarP 
namo 'stu dharmāya vadanpraviśya jalaṃ sa me prīta iti kṣipecca 
snātvā tatastīrthavaṭākṣayaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā pradadyādatha dakṣiṇāṃ tu  NarP 
evaṃ kṛtvā pretapure sthitasya svarge gatiḥ syātta mahendratulyā  NarP 
pravāhamavadhiṃ kṛtvā yāvaddhastacatuṣṭayam 
tatra nārāyaṇaḥ svāmī nānyaḥ svāmī kadācana  NarP 
na tatra pratigṛhṇīyātprāṇaiḥ kaṇṭhagatairapi 
bhādraśuklacaturdaśyāṃ yāvadākramate jalam  NarP 
tāvadgabhaṃ vijānīyāttaddūraṃ tīramucyate 
sārddhahastaśataṃ yāvadgarbhastīraṃ tataḥ param  NarP 
iti keṣāṃ mataṃ devi śrutismṛtiṣu saṃmatam 
tīrādgavyūtimātraṃ tu paritaḥ kṣetramucyate  NarP 
tīraṃ tyaktvā vasetkṣetre tīre vāso na ceṣyate 
ekayojanavistīrṇā kṣetrasīmā taṭadvayāt  NarP 
gaṅgāsīmāṃ na laghanti pāpānyapyakhilānyapi 
tāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā palāyante yathā siṃhaṃ vanaukasaḥ  NarP 
yatra gaṅgā mahābhāge rāmaśaṃbhutapovanam 
siddhakṣetraṃ tu tajjñeyaṃ samantāttu triyojanam  NarP 
tīrthe na pratigṛhṇīyātpuṇyeṣvāyataneṣu ca 
nimitteṣu ca sarveṣu tannivṛtto bhavennaraḥ  NarP 
tīrthe yaḥ pratigṛhṇāti puṇyeṣvāyataneṣu ca 
niṣphalaṃ tasya tattīrthaṃ yāvattaddhanamucyate  NarP 
gaṅgāvikrayāṇāddevi viṣṇorvikrayaṇaṃ bhavet 
janārdane tu vikrīte vikrītaṃ bhuvanatrayam  NarP 
gaṅgā tīrasamudbhūtāṃ madaṃ mūrghnā bibharti yaḥ 
bibharti rūpaṃ sor'kasya tamonāśāya kevalam  NarP 
gaṅgāpulinajāṃ dhūlimāstīryātha nijān pitṝn 
prīṇayanyo naraḥ piṇḍāndadyāttān svarnayedapi  NarP 
idaṃ te 'bhihitaṃ bhadre gaṅgāmāhātmyamuttamam 
paṭhan śṛṇvannaro hyeti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  NarP 
nityaṃ japyamidaṃ bhaktyā prayataiḥ śraddhayānvitaiḥ 
vaiṣṇavīṃ gatimicchadbhiḥ śaivīṃ vā vidhinandini  NarP 
iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīvasusaṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye pūjādikathaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
